Hawaii's Bid to Become a U.S. State; American Federation of Labor Strongly Opposes; This Move Would Give Japanese Residents the Opportunity to Join the Senate 51

Honolulu The efforts of local leaders to seek statehood for Hawaii suffered a setback today when the American Federation of Labor decided to use all of the Labor Party's power in Congress to oppose the passage of the proposal to make Hawaii a state. It is rumored that the AFL is concerned that because Hawaii has a large Asian population, two Japanese residents of the island would be able to become senators in the Washington Congress after the proposal is passed. (26th Reuters Telegram)

New Zealand Election; Government Defeated by Labor Party; First Time in History 52

Wellington, New Zealand In today's general election in New Zealand, the National Government led by Prime Minister Forbes and Finance Minister Coates was heavily defeated by the Labor Party. This Labor victory is a first in New Zealand history. The Labor Party not only retained its existing seats but also won many seats in key government districts. The government's defeat was largely due to the newly formed Democratic Party fielding separate candidates, which split the government's forces. Currently, the number of seats won by each party is as follows, excluding seven unknown seats: Labor Party 48 seats, Government 17 seats, Independents 8 seats. The composition of the previous House of Representatives was as follows: Government Party 47 seats, Labor Party 24 seats, Independents 9 seats. (27th Reuters Telegram)

Wellington, New Zealand New Zealand is scheduled to hold a general election tomorrow. The 76 seats in the House of Representatives occupied by Europeans will be contested. Today, the Maori people elected four Maori members of parliament, including the former Native Affairs Officer, Mr. Ngata. It should be noted that the current government is composed of a mixed party (Reform Party 28 members, United Party 19 members), totaling 47 seats. The opposition party, the Labor Party, occupies 24 seats. The current government is campaigning on a platform of seeking recovery through financial stability, while the opposition party advocates guaranteed commodity prices and national control of loans and currency. (26th Reuters Telegram)

Egyptian Parties Differ on Constitutional Issues; Internal Strife Inevitable 53

Cairo The Nationalist Party recently issued a declaration criticizing Mamelouk, the leader of the Liberal Constitutionalist Party. Other parties are demanding the restoration of the 1923 Constitution and using it as a common political platform. The Liberal Constitutionalist Party refused to cooperate, which is incorrect. After the declaration was issued, the People's Party, the Liberal Constitutionalist Party, and the Nationalist Party's splinter faction all decided to issue separate declarations to explain each party's position on constitutional issues. It is generally believed that the parties' diverging views will inevitably lead to internal strife, causing general political issues to take a back seat. As for Prime Minister Nessim, although his health is weak, he still intends to continue serving in the central government, believing that the current government must calmly deal with the situation if domestic security is to be maintained and some concessions are to be obtained from Britain. It remains uncertain whether a cabinet crisis will erupt. (27th Havas Telegram)

On the Eve of the Reopening of the French Parliament; Laval Delivers a Speech on Domestic and Foreign Affairs; Maintaining Economic Balance and Opposing Currency Devaluation; Safeguarding the Republican System and Strictly Controlling Violent Groups; Maintaining Friendly Cooperation with Britain on the Italy-Abyssinia Issue; Emphasizing Good Neighborliness and Consolidating European Peace with Italy 54

(Paris) The French Senate and Chamber of Deputies have ended their recess and will reconvene tomorrow. As is customary before the parliament's resumption, the Prime Minister will deliver a speech outlining the government's views. Therefore, Prime Minister Laval delivered a radio broadcast speech tonight, addressing domestic issues such as financial problems, the franc issue, and the fascist groups issue, as well as foreign affairs such as the Italy-Abyssinia issue and collective security. The speech was quite lengthy, and excerpts are provided below:

Laval first addressed the franc issue, stating that the first thing to be decided when the parliament reconvenes on Thursday is the fate of the franc. "How to maintain economic balance and avoid currency devaluation is the most pressing task. If the parliament opposes this view, it should clearly state so, as the people have the inherent right to understand the situation. Otherwise, if parliamentarians argue endlessly, it will inevitably create a state of uncertainty and fatally damage finances. Therefore, the current plan is to ask the parliament to vote on the financial issues quickly and without delay, or the consequences will be unimaginable."

He then explained the legitimacy of the government's legislative orders, stating that the government has always opposed currency devaluation, as it directly increases the burden on modest and poor families, which is very dangerous. It is particularly inappropriate to implement it today, when the general parliamentary elections are approaching. Therefore, the government is determined to resolutely reject it, said Laval. Laval continued that after the financial issues are resolved, the parliament may discuss the issue of so-called fascist groups, for which the government is also prepared. "Guaranteeing the safety of citizens and safeguarding the republican system are the government's responsibilities. No matter which party or faction, if it wants to abuse its power and replace the authority of the state with the authority of the party, it is not allowed by law. Events such as the Brest and Toulon incidents, and the recent clashes between the Croix-de-Feu and the Popular Front in Limoges, are all violations of the law. If such incidents occur again in the future, the government will cause the groups participating in these incidents to lose their right to freedom. Existing laws, if inadequate, will be supplemented by the government. In any case, the government will ensure that everyone abides by the law before it is over. Everyone knows that I have always loved peace, so I especially hope that peace should start from within the country. Violence, no matter where it comes from, is opposed by me. I dare to tell the people not to disturb themselves unnecessarily, so as not to please the enemies. For example, on November 11th this year, people from both the left and right factions demonstrated separately in front of the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier, fellow countrymen confronting each other. What is this if not the seeds of chaos? How can people believe in our great nation if it does not know how to rein itself in? In short, national unity is the only way to save the country."

Laval then discussed the Italy-Abyssinia issue, stating that "international conventions are a major factor in our country's security, so we have an obligation to fulfill the results produced by the conventions. On the one hand, we seek long-term cooperation with Britain, and on the other hand, we always want to find ways to localize the dispute. We have exhausted everything to avoid the expansion of the conflict. Since the beginning of the Italy-Abyssinia conflict, we have always advocated avoiding military sanctions. Measures sufficient to cause a naval blockade and the closure of the Suez Canal have never been considered. The task I have undertaken is very difficult, because on the one hand, I must always maintain friendly cooperation with Britain and show that France abides by the League of Nations covenant, and on the other hand, I must maintain friendship with Italy. The reason why I do not avoid difficulties and mediate between the two is simply to ensure that our country's own interests and peace can be taken care of on both sides. I have been looking for a friendly solution to the Italy-Abyssinia conflict with unwavering perseverance. There is no fault to be found in this attempt, because sanctions are not the only strategy to stop the war. The cooperation between Britain and France should be as close and sincere as possible, even more so than in the past, because what Britain and France jointly seek is nothing more than peace. For the sake of preserving peace, Britain and France are united in thought and deed, without the slightest gap between them. What we hope is that once the opportunity comes, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will change his mind, so that our efforts to mediate the Italy-Abyssinia dispute will not be in vain. The Italy-Abyssinia dispute must find an honorable and just solution, on the one hand respecting the principles of the League of Nations, and on the other hand taking into account Italy's interests. I believe that responsible people around the world will share this sentiment. I believe that the leaders of the Italian government must deeply desire to have Italy rejoin the European peace organization, in which case the work started by the Stresa Front at that time may not be impossible to continue." Finally, Laval talked about collective security, briefly stating that "France has always adhered to the principle of collective security, and in any case," that is, regarding the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact, there is absolutely no intention to oppose any country. This has recently been repeatedly stated to German leader Hitler by French Ambassador to Germany, François-Poncet. In short, we do not abandon any friendship, we respect all constraints, and we strive for cooperation among all countries to jointly consolidate European peace. As for Germany, we especially sincerely hope to establish and develop good neighborly relations of mutual respect, because France, as a strong, vibrant, and peace-loving country, has nothing to fear." (26th Havas Telegram)

The Fate of the French Cabinet Hinges on Two Current Issues; Fascist Organizations and Financial Issues; Left-Wing Meeting Fails to Reach a Compromise 55

(Paris) Today's meeting of left-wing parties failed to reach a compromise on the debate at tomorrow's parliamentary session, giving Laval hope of winning the political storm. Therefore, the stock exchange's sentiment turned strong, and the price of public bonds rose by three-quarters of a pound sterling in half an hour, and the price of francs was also stronger. The left-wing parties will continue to meet tomorrow in an attempt to reach a common ground to overthrow the government. The Radical Party advocates that according to Laval's request, the issue of the franc should be discussed first when the parliament opens tomorrow. If the government can first win the financial debate, it can then deal with the Fascist case with more certainty. At today's meeting of the left-wing parties, someone asked Socialist leader Blum what he would do if the government was overthrown tomorrow. Blum said that he would form a government within two hours that was sure to dissolve all Fascist organizations. (27th Reuters Telegram)

(Paris) The Radical Socialist Party's parliamentary group recently passed a resolution adopting Prime Minister Laval's proposal to first discuss the government's financial policy when the parliament reconvenes, and then immediately continue to discuss the issue of Fascist groups. If this resolution is passed by a majority in the parliament, the political storm can be temporarily eased. However, the parliament has 160 Radical Party members, and the above-mentioned group resolution was only passed by a majority of 28 votes to 20 votes, which is extremely noteworthy. Also, at this morning's State Council meeting, the cabinet members resolutely stated that the government should do everything possible to curb the improper activities of Fascist groups, a move that on the surface is quite sufficient to ease the political tension. (26th Havas Telegram)

(Paris) The French Parliament will meet on Thursday, and this meeting will likely be one of the most important scenes in the history of the Third Republic. The current issue not only concerns the survival of the Laval Cabinet, but also greatly relates to the French democratic system itself. The opinions of the left and right wings in the Parliament on various important domestic and foreign issues are more disparate than before. The biggest points of contention in domestic affairs are approximately three: (1) Dissolving right-wing Fascist organizations, such as the Croix-de-Feu, the French Action, and the Patriotic League, which is not only urgently demanded by the Socialist, Communist, and Popular Front, but also firmly advocated by the most powerful Acute Socialist Party in the Parliament. (2) Laval's cabinet's financial and economic policies, Laval has tried his best to reduce the salaries of government personnel, the pensions of veterans, and administrative expenses, and has achieved the goal of budget balance, but whether it should continue is also a question. (3) The issue of controlling the parliamentary re-election in May next year. As for foreign affairs, although France's current position is very complicated, and its relations with the whole world are very important, observers believe that this is only a secondary issue. The situation of the left and right factions in the parliament: the left seems to be uniting, led by Independent Deputy Henriot or even former left-leaning Prime Minister Paul-Boncour, and using the Fascist organization issue or financial issues as weapons to overthrow Laval. The Socialist Party today has resolved to contact other left-wing organizations to overthrow the current cabinet, so the situation has become more serious. As a result, an unusual force may emerge in the French political circles and seize power. For example, the Croix-de-Feu claims to have 300,000 members. According to the left, the group has received instructions to incite a coup. The biggest difficulty for the current government is the government's civil servants, because they are well-organized and have long been known as "a country within a country," and their political views are quite close to the left wing. Therefore, their power should not be underestimated when the left attacks the government in the future. (26th National Telegram)

(Paris) A senior official of the Bank of France told an Associated Press reporter today that there is no reason to panic, and the franc is not in danger of devaluation, and there is no possibility of a financial crisis. However, according to the bank's report, approximately 4,500,000,000 francs of gold flowed out in the first twenty-four days of November. (26th National Telegram)

Opening of the New British Parliament; Members of the House of Commons Sworn In; FitzRoy Re-Elected as Speaker 56

(London) The new parliament opened this afternoon, and Conservative MP FitzRoy was elected as Speaker, his fourth re-election as Speaker. Prime Minister Baldwin, Leader of the Opposition in the House of Commons Attlee, and "Father of the House" Lloyd George, former Prime Minister during the European War, all extended their warm congratulations. FitzRoy said in his speech that the reason why the parliamentary system is so noble is that the whole country deeply believes that all public opinions in the country have the opportunity to be expressed fairly and freely. He intends to maintain the freedom of speech that makes the position and reputation of the British Parliament admired by the world. FitzRoy continued that he had repeatedly urged members to be concise in their speeches. A debate is valuable for its concise nature. If it is solely for the purpose of eloquent speeches, it loses the true meaning of the debate. If this continues unchanged, it will reduce the public's interest in parliamentary discussions. After FitzRoy finished his speech, the members were sworn in. (26th Reuters Telegram)

(London) Liberal MPs in the House of Commons met today and elected Sinclair as leader to replace the defeated Samuel. Lloyd George also attended the meeting. According to congressional reporters for various newspapers, Lloyd George and members of the Independent Liberal Party in the previous House of Commons will cooperate with members of the party in the new House of Commons, so the unified Liberal Party can reach 21 seats. (26th Reuters Telegram)

(London) It should be noted that Sinclair is a member elected from northern Scotland. He served as Secretary of State for Scotland in the early days of the MacDonald Cabinet. Later, he disagreed with Conservative cabinet members and resigned together with his party's Interior Minister, Sir Samuel. After Samuel was defeated in the recent House of Commons re-election, he was unable to serve as chairman of the party group. Also, because Lloyd George was humble, Sinclair was elected. As for Lloyd George, for the past five years, he has been the leader of the independent Liberal Party in the opposition. He is now cooperating with the orthodox Liberal Party again, as can be seen from his assuming the chairmanship of the Liberal Party group meeting. (26th Havas Telegram)

Pacific Chamber of Commerce to Meet in Honolulu 58

Honolulu The Western Branch of the US Chamber of Commerce will hold its annual meeting here on Wednesday. Attendees will include President Eberle and 300 others. Representatives from China, Japan, Australia, New Zealand, and other Pacific countries have arrived here. (26th National Radio)

The Inside Story of Yin Rugeng's Establishment of a Puppet Organization: Forcibly Incorporating Yanqing, Xianghe, and Other Counties into the Demilitarized Zone; Seeking Instructions from a Certain Country's Military Attache Regarding Dismissal Orders; Song Zheyuan and Others Return from Tianjin to Beiping to Maintain Order 59

Beiping Correspondence: The Hebei situation has seen much brewing recently. However, due to the authorities' calm approach, the extent of the developments is considerably different from what is reported in Japanese newspapers. However, Yin Rugeng, the Administrative Inspector of the Luantung and Jiyu Districts, claiming his situation was exceptional, issued an absurd circular telegram, far beyond general expectations. Song Zheyuan even telegraphed Yin about this matter, urging him to be cautious and not act rashly. Yin then went to Tianjin to reside, rarely meeting with visiting guests. Initially, it was unexpected that Yin would declare his betrayal of the motherland at midnight on the 25th, establishing the so-called "Jidong Anti-Communist Autonomous Committee" puppet organization in Tong County, publishing a proclamation to the people, an inaugural declaration, and telegrams to Song, Han, and others. As for this puppet organization, it has nine committee members, with Yin as the puppet chairman. His excuse is that he is breaking away from the central government based on the Tanggu Truce and implementing people's autonomy. The so-called committee members claim to have been elected by the War Zone Autonomy Promotion Association. The puppet committee internally has seven departments: Puppet Foreign Affairs Director Huo Shi, Puppet Civil Affairs Director Zhang Renli, Puppet Secretariat Director Zhang (concurrent), Puppet Finance Director Zhao Congyi, Puppet Construction Director Wang Xiacai, and Puppet Security Director Dong Fengxiang. As for the original counties under the Luantung and Jiyu Districts, the Aoyu District includes Linyu, Funing, Changli, Qian'an, Lulong, Luan County, Leting, and Fengrun, totaling eight counties. The Jiyu District includes Zunhua, Xinglong, Yutian, Pinggu, Miyun, Huairou, Sanhe, Ji County, Shunyi, and Tong County, totaling ten counties. It is rumored that Yin Rugeng is preparing to incorporate neighboring counties of the "War Zone" such as Yanqing, Changping, Xianghe, Baozhi, Ninghe, Wuqing, Anshun, and other seven counties into his jurisdiction. It is evident that Yin's rebellious actions are unrestrained.

When the so-called "Jidong Anti-Communist Autonomous Committee" puppet organization was established in Tongzhou on the 25th, over thirty foreign reporters were present. Among them, the British and American reporters were the most emotionally charged. Chinese reporters, although maintaining composure, mostly revealed infinite emotion. Japanese reporters, on the other hand, were extremely busy. A portion of them mingled with the Chinese and foreign reporters to listen to Yin's speech, while the majority were in Yin's office, conducting special interviews. After the so-called inauguration ceremony, Yin, accompanied by a Japanese advisor, went to the reception room to meet the reporters, speaking shamelessly, unaware that he himself had become a slave to others. At the time, someone asked Yin why such a grand ceremony had no flags representing the political system, and isn't that strange? Yin replied that it was unnecessary. A certain foreign reporter then sarcastically said in French, "Even bandits have flags, what about your esteemed association?" When Yin spoke about the tasks of the puppet committee, he became carried away and said that he wanted (Yin arbitrarily incorporated the four counties of Changping, Xianghe, Ninghe, and Ningdi, which were close to the "War Zone") to create a district of the Kingly Way Paradise. At this time, someone immediately asked Yin whether the financial resources of the twenty-two counties could achieve satisfactory goals. Yin replied that there are over a thousand "esteemed" counties. When asked what the total area of the twenty-two counties was, Yin was speechless, embarrassedly replying that everyone could check the map. Finally, Yin also said that they were breaking away from party rule, not leaving China, and that everyone should recognize the topic. At this point, the Japanese advisor urged Yin to leave. Chinese and foreign reporters also returned to Beiping.

On the day that Yin and others rebelled in Tongzhou, Tianjin was also suddenly tense. Several hundred drug-addicted vagrants falsely claimed to be representatives of a petition for autonomy. Fortunately, the authorities took effective precautions, and the Japanese did not provide them with support, so the situation was quelled on the same day. During the petition, the drug-addicted vagrants wore yellow uniforms and lotus-leaf hats, looking bizarre and only able to frighten merchants and residents. By evening, when they were disarmed and dismissed, their true colors were revealed, and they were in a miserable state. Song Zheyuan, the commander of the Pingjin Garrison, who was briefly resting in Tianjin, returned to Beiping on the evening of the 25th to take charge. Qin Decun, the mayor of Beiping, and Xiao Zhenying, the chairman of Chahar Province, represented the authorities in informing the press that within the scope of the 29th Army's power, there would be absolutely no problems with local security. Therefore, the people of Beiping are still trending toward stability.

Regarding Hebei diplomacy, recent reports from various sources all confirm that a decision has been made by the central government. The saying that He Yingqin would come north to preside over political affairs had been widely spread a week ago. Since the news of the Executive Yuan's decision today (26th) to specially appoint He as the director of the Executive Yuan's Beiping Office arrived in Beiping, the emotions of all parties have been uplifted, unanimously considering it a gratifying event. Zhu Zheyuan and others, who have been struggling for a month, also indirectly indicated to others that the current situation in the north has hope for smooth development due to He's imminent arrival in the north. Song will assume his new position as Director of the Ji-Cha Pacification Headquarters after He arrives in Beiping. At that time, the Pingjin Garrison Headquarters may be abolished. More than ten important figures in the Beiping education community, including Jiang Menglin, Mei Yi-qi, and Hu Shi, visited Song Zheyuan at his residence in Wuyiku Hutong at 2:00 PM today (26th) due to the current situation, and only left around 6:00 PM. According to Hu Shi's statement to reporters, he considered the meeting with Song to be satisfactory. This shows that all the external rumors are not true. During the conversation, he expressed admiration for Song's spirit of struggling through the difficult situation and said that all rumors could be dispelled without attack. After the Executive Yuan's order to dismiss Yin Rugeng and bring him to justice arrived in Beiping, the traitor Yin made a phone call from Tong County to a certain country's military attache to ask for instructions. A special Japanese train left Shanhaiguan this morning (26th) and stopped briefly in Luan County around 7:00 AM. It did not delay when passing through Tianjin and arrived in Beiping at 3:00 PM in the afternoon. Xiao Zhenying, the chairman of Chahar Province, and Qin Decun, the mayor of Beiping, went to Tianjin a few days ago to negotiate with various parties on ways to develop the situation. At 1:30 PM on the 25th, they returned to Beiping from Tianjin by car with Song Zheyuan, the commander of the Pingjin Garrison. They did not stop when passing through Tong County and arrived in Beiping at 5:40 PM. Because Beiping is near Tianjin, and disturbances occurred in Tianjin, the people of Beiping were naturally uneasy. Therefore, security has now been tightened. After Yin Rugeng announced the establishment of the puppet organization, the county magistrates were extremely dissatisfied with Yin and returned to Baoding one after another. The magistrates of Linyu and Leting counties have arrived in Baoding to ask for instructions from the provincial government. The Hebei Provincial Government is quite calm about this incident, believing that it has no significant impact on the overall situation in North China. In addition to telegraphing the central government for instructions, it has ordered the county magistrates and security brigade commanders to fulfill their duties and do their best to maintain local security.

After the establishment of the puppet Jidong Anti-Communist Committee, the ambassadors, ministers, and charge d'affaires of various countries in China telegraphed their respective countries to report the truth. After receiving the telegrams from Yin Rugeng and others, the central government repeatedly telegraphed Beiping to inquire about the process. The Beiping authorities are fully responsible for security. However, tonight (26th) at 9:00 PM, trams were taken off the tracks early, and the military police began inspecting pedestrians at 10:00 PM. (26th)

Tianjin Once Experienced Disturbances: Those Claiming to Be Representatives of the People Petitioned, Occupied the Lecture Hall, and Formed a Suicide Squad 60

Tianjin Correspondence: Rumors have been rife here since January, and society has been uneasy. Unexpectedly, on the 22nd, those claiming to be so-called citizen representatives attempted to hold a meeting but failed. However, four people went directly to the municipal government to petition, demanding that Mayor Cheng Ke return power to the people and implement autonomy. On the 24th, five-color leaflets were found distributed in the thoroughfares. On the same day, the so-called "Puan Association" posted slogans and declarations, the wording of which was nothing more than Japan-Manchuria-China united, realizing Greater Asianism, and uniting the members of the National Anqing Gang. That night, it was rumored that plainclothes teams would depart from a certain place, wearing police uniforms, numbering over a thousand people. The Public Security Bureau, upon learning of this, temporarily ordered the police on duty in each district to wear summer police hats so that they could be easily identified when action was taken. Security was maintained throughout the night, so it was passed safely. Unexpectedly, at around 6:00 AM on the 25th, more than ten trucks suddenly drove out of a certain concession, with red and white cloth banners hanging all over the trucks. The trucks carried over a hundred people wearing grass-green uniforms, yellow soft hats, red five-pointed star badges, short wooden sticks, and dry food bags and kettles. They also carried two portable machine guns and two machine guns. They drove to the First Popular Lecture Hall on Dongma Road, smashed open the door, and all entered. They immediately hung red cloth outside the door, with the words "North China People's Self-Defense Corps Suicide Squad" written on it. There was also white cloth with the words "North China People's Self-Defense Corps Headquarters" written on it. Machine guns were set up in the thoroughfare. Soon, over two hundred people in plainclothes, with cloth badges of the fake North China People's Self-Defense Corps wrapped around their arms and holding cloth flags with slogans, also arrived at the hall to gather. Protected by those in uniform, they boarded more than ten trucks, led by a certain foreigner in a car, and traveled along Dahu Tong to Jingang Bridge. Several people in uniform jumped down first and went to the east and west yamen of the Tianjin-Gugu Security Headquarters, standing like guards. The rest rushed to the New Railway Station along Dajing Road, parading and demonstrating along the way, shouting slogans. After getting off at the New Railway Station, the people were divided into several groups. The first group, about twenty people in uniform and forty in plainclothes, took two cars directly to the municipal government on Yuewei Road, demanding to see the mayor. Mayor Cheng Ke had not yet arrived. Secretary-General Sun Runyu rushed from his residence upon hearing the report. It was 8:40 AM. When asked about their intentions, over twenty people in plainclothes and eight in uniform entered and claimed to Sun that they had come to petition for autonomy and return power to the people. When asked about the names of their group and representatives, they replied that they were the North China People's Self-Help Corps, and the representatives were Wu Meixiang, Wu Wenru, and Wang Zhupo. Sun agreed to convey their intentions to the mayor. At this time, another group of about a hundred people in plainclothes also came to petition. The municipal government sent people to persuade them to leave. However, the eight people in uniform refused to leave the municipal government's reception room. Sun telegraphed Ikeshang, the captain of the Japanese gendarmerie, to come with two gendarmes to help drive them away. At around 10:00 AM, the so-called Cangxian People's Self-Defense Corps, all in plainclothes, numbering about a hundred people, continued to arrive at the municipal government. Sun sent someone to meet with them. The petitioners refused to send representatives inside. The Security Department had no choice but to send out special armed forces to guard the area, dragging six of their leaders inside. Wang Xinggang interrogated them about their intentions. The six people cried for help. The soldiers were extremely angry and surrounded Wang, asking the adjutant to punish these people. Wang then telephoned Shang Zhen in Baoding to ask for instructions. He received a reply, instructing him to handle it properly immediately. Ikeshang, the captain of the Japanese gendarmerie, also received the news and demanded the release of the six people by telephone. After the release, the petitioners gathered outside the door and dispersed. However, dozens of members of the suicide squad occupying the lecture hall refused to retreat, displaying six or seven large trucks on the street and distributing leaflets, which were signed "North China Autonomy Petition Group," "Wang Ming, Commander of the North China Self-Defense Corps," and "Tian Zhiping, Captain of the North China People's Self-Defense Corps Suicide Squad." The police were unable to stop them. Mayor Cheng Ke and Public Security Bureau Chief Liu Yushu contacted various parties from morning to afternoon and met with Tada, the commander of the Japanese army, Ohyan, the newly established head of the Kwantung Army's Tianjin special service agency, and Doihara, asking them to assist in resolving the situation with the maintenance of security in mind. By 5:00 PM, they obtained the consent of the Japanese side, and several gendarmes were dispatched to assist the special service team and the personnel of the First Branch Bureau of the Public Security Bureau to go to the lecture hall to persuade the so-called suicide squad captain to leave. The members of the team were all recruited temporarily, unkempt and with long hair. They occupied the lecture hall and prepared their own cooking utensils, roasting steamed buns with pickles and eating heartily. When someone entered and asked who their leader was, they replied that they did not know. When asked what they planned to do, they replied that they were following orders. When asked anything else, they were completely ignorant. When they were persuaded to leave, most of them took off their uniforms and scattered quietly. The people who claimed to be the petition group were mostly servants hired from various pawnshops to carry ceremonial weapons, paid four cents a day. From 10:00 PM on the 25th, the entire city was under martial law, and no one was allowed to pass through. As of the 26th, it was still under heavy guard. (26th)

Songjiang: Red Cross Telegraphed Province Requesting Ban on Quarrying 61

Zhou Xuewen, the chairman of the Songjiang branch of the Chinese Red Cross, stated that the Jiufeng Mountains in Songjiang Prefecture are natural scenic spots and historical sites, especially with many tombs of famous figures from past dynasties, as recorded in local chronicles. Since the national government established its capital, local ruffians, driven by greed, have used afforestation and land reclamation as pretexts to fraudulently obtain mountain land licenses, actually implementing their scheme to destroy graves and exhume tombs for profit. Skeletal remains are scattered, a tragic sight to behold. Recently, due to the imperfect organization of factories, the various quarrying factories have successively closed down, and the unemployed workers are suffering from hunger and cold. Moreover, many are immigrants, making it easy to cause trouble. For the sake of local security, it is especially important to repatriate them early. The Red Cross has telegraphed the Civil Affairs Department of the Provincial Government, requesting that the aforementioned workers be repatriated immediately and consulting the Ministries of Railways and Communications to issue passports and provide free transportation. It also hopes that the county will be ordered to ban the illegal quarrying of the Jiufeng Mountains. The Provincial Department has now approved the instructions, stating that the telegram has been received, and the county should be ordered to strictly enforce the ban and consult with the Ministries of Communications and Railways for investigation and handling.

The Wuxian Public Security Bureau has implemented the opening of public prostitution, designated areas for public prostitution, and begun the registration of public prostitutes. There are also several dozen variant prostitutes, the Minsheng singing girls, who should register as first-class, but because they do not want to sell their bodies, they have not yet registered. Next month, syphilis examinations will be conducted on the prostitutes, and prostitution licenses will be issued. The official opening will be on New Year's Day next year.

Wuxi: Autumn Harvest Reduced by Seven Percent Throughout the County 63

The autumn rice in the four rural districts of this county has been affected by white spider mites, resulting in a significant reduction in harvest. The Provincial Committee has already surveyed and reported this. It is now learned that the percentage of general reduction has been determined by the Jiangsu Finance Department. In the Liu Cangxiang Township of the Fifth District and the Yanchao Town's Wusan, Wu Si, Wu Wu, Wu Liu, and San Tu areas, one percent has been added, changing the general reduction to six percent, with an actual collection of four percent. In the Beiqifang Town's Liuyi and Liuer areas of the Ninth District, one percent has been added, changing the general reduction to five percent, with an actual collection of five percent. In the remaining fields throughout the county, three li have been added, changing the general reduction to seven percent, with an actual collection of nine percent and three li. Yesterday, the Finance Department instructed the county government to issue a public announcement, and all tenant farmers throughout the county should comply and pay accordingly.

Changzhou: Villager Robbed and Shot Midway 64

Zhong Hexi, a farmer near Xunyan Bridge in the Eighth District of Wuyi, traveled to the city with neighbors on the 26th by Wuyi bus to pay taxes. At around 5:00 PM, he took the bus back to his hometown, but he had to walk more than ten li to get home after getting off the bus in Caoqiao Town. Unexpectedly, when he reached the Magou Shang area, a robber wearing a woolen coat and a duckbill hat, holding a box gun, shouted for him to stop. Axi pleaded with him, saying that all his silver dollars had been used to pay taxes. The robber did not believe him and forcibly searched him. Axi resisted, and the robber shot him in the left hand. Neighbors reported to the nearby security team, who rushed to pursue and arrest the perpetrator. Axi, who was injured, was carried to the Wujin Hospital in the city the next day. Fortunately, the injury was minor and should not be a major problem.

All new and old roads in the provincial capital will be replanted with trees.

Hangzhou: Surveying Oujiang to Be Completed by the End of the Year 66

The Zhejiang Construction Department approved the letter from the Ouhai Customs Supervisory Office, stating that if the Oujiang River is silted up, and there is a need to collect surcharges on imported goods through the Customs to be used as dredging expenses, a detailed plan for dredging the river and the required amount of expenses should be prepared, and the applicable surcharge rate and the number of years required should be estimated based on the Customs' three-year tax revenue situation. It ordered the Water Conservancy Bureau to quickly survey and estimate the expenses to be submitted for review. The Bureau is now actively processing the surveying, and it can all be completed by the end of the year. A budget for the dredging project will be prepared and submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval.

Artistic Talk

Concrete Beauty 69

— Feng Zikai

When listening to people speak, concrete, trivial, and simple statements often sound more pleasing than abstract, grand, and profound ones. Let me first give a most obvious example: saying "the problem of livelihood" is not as pleasing as saying "the problem of clothing and food"; saying "the problem of clothing and food" is not as pleasing as saying "the problem of rice bowls" or "the problem of bread." Because the word "livelihood" encompasses everything comprehensively, it is too abstract, too grand, and too profound, so listeners do not gain a deep understanding, a strong impression, or a strong interest from it. If you change it to the three words "clothing and food," because it is more concrete, more trivial, and more simple, listeners find it easier to understand, the impression is strong and clear, and it is full of interest and can be grasped. Sometimes, speakers even feel that the words "clothing and food" are too broad, so they go a step further and use the words "rice bowl" or "bread." These are the most common and familiar objects to everyone, and who doesn't immediately gain a personal interest, a strong impression, and a full understanding when they hear them? Therefore, "unemployment" is often translated as "smashing the rice bowl"; "loss of land" is also translated as "changing the color of the map," making listeners shocked.

I now call this speaking technique "concrete beauty." This is also one of the rhetorical devices after the progress of human language, similar to the "metaphor" I discussed earlier (the article was published in a certain issue of a literary magazine this year), but there are differences: metaphor also uses concrete things to help reason; however, the concrete object taken has no relationship with reasoning itself, only the same nature. For example, "Why use an ox-cleaver to kill a chicken?" This matter has nothing to do with Confucius's way of governing, only the nature of "using great talent for a small task" is the same, so it is cited as a metaphor to make reasoning concrete and interesting, and easier to listen to. The "concrete beauty" discussed now is different: the concrete object taken must have a close relationship with reasoning, so that listeners can see the big in the small and the whole in the part. For example, "rice bowl" or "bread" has a close relationship with "livelihood," and is the most important part or core of "livelihood." Therefore, the speaker only needs to give this one corner, and the listeners can infer three, ten, a hundred, or a thousand. The so-called "rice bowl" actually includes everything edible, such as old wine, cigarettes, and lighters. I think this language technique is most meaningful, especially when listening to lectures and reading papers. A long and broad abstract principle often makes people headache or sleepy. On the contrary, if you make good use of metaphors and this kind of concrete beauty, listeners will not feel tired; if you make good use of it, a few words can be worth tens of thousands of words. The speeches of those who advised, such as Chun Yukun and Dongfang Shuo, and the speeches of poets can be said to be examples of this.

There are countless examples of this kind of concrete beauty in our daily language and in poetry. For the convenience of savoring, I will excerpt a few that I can think of below, but this is just one corner.

Throwing down the pen, volunteering for service, removing armor, dismounting, resigning from office, ascending the throne, dusting off one's hat, binding one's hair, washing one's ears, wiping one's eyes, retiring from office, mourning for the dead, shaving one's head, making a living, sweeping the couch, holding the bull's ear, seizing the championship banner, holding the teaching whip, following in the footsteps, sleeping soundly, living freely in the forest, bowing down under the skirt, fighting to offer clogs,...

Literally speaking, most of these words don't make sense. Do scholars hold pens day and night? Do warriors never remove their armor day and night? Those who abandon their official positions often live in concessions, why resign from office? Does any leader hold a bull's ear in his hand? However, this is where the interest of concrete beauty lies. Some of them rely on the help of classics or are close to metaphors. But the principle is always to see the big in the small and the whole in the part. There are also many good examples of this in colloquial language. The mouths of those who are good at speaking often reveal them. They don't say "a certain family has no food to eat," they say "the bottom of a certain family's pot is facing the sky." They don't say "a certain person can be famous in later generations," they say "a certain person will eat cold leftovers." Chuan Baicun said that the women's problem is the problem of "stomach and uterus." Wu Zhihui said that love is "sperm acting strangely." Although the language is harsh, it is pleasing to hear. It can be said to have exhausted the ability to concretize language. Unfortunately, my knowledge is too narrow and my memory is too bad to think of more examples for a while. (To be continued)

Local News

Three Organizations Telegraph for the Suppression of the Hebei-East Rebels, Requesting He Yingqin to Immediately Go North to Be Stationed in Tianjin and Beijing, Declaring Opposition to Any Autonomous Organization in North China 70

The Citizen's Federation of the First Special District of this city and the Chinese General Federation of Industry telegraphed to the central government and the generals of North China yesterday, requesting the suppression of the pseudo-Hebei-East Anti-Communist Autonomous Council. The United Federation of Universities telegraphed to the authorities in Beijing and North China yesterday, requesting a quick punishment and suppression, and telegraphed to the authorities of various countries, declaring the meaning of opposition. The following is an excerpt of the original text.

Telegraph to the Central Government: The City Federation telegraphed to the Central Government, saying: Nanjing Central Executive Committee, National Government Executive Yuan, Military Affairs Committee, [all recipients] Jian, Yin Rugeng, used by others, dared to lead twenty-two counties in Hebei-East to establish the so-called Hebei-East Anti-Communist Autonomous Committee in Tong County, using the pretext of public opinion to destroy the integrity of our country's territory. The news spread, and we were deeply indignant. We believe that Yin is the Administrative Inspector Commissioner of the Ji-Mi District, and should do his best to be loyal and jointly defend the country. Unexpectedly, he did not think about this plan, but colluded with traitors, served as a pawn, and was so insane. Fortunately, our central government has insight into the traitorous situation and has clearly ordered his dismissal and arrest, upholding justice and saving the people from fire and water. Now, the people of Hebei-East urgently hope that our central government will send senior officials to comfort them and quell the chaos. We hereby telegraph, please forward to He Yingqin, the Chief of the Executive Yuan's Office in Beiping, to go north immediately to be stationed in Tianjin and Beijing, and lay the foundation for the country. We are extremely eager to receive this, (2) The Chinese General Federation of Industry telegraphed to the Central Government, saying: Nanjing National Government, Executive Yuan, Military Affairs Committee, [all recipients] Jian, In recent years, the situation of our China has been subjected to strong pressure from outside and harassment by traitors from within. Sometimes, they do not hesitate to sacrifice national honor to please foreigners and become puppets, which is extremely insane. Now, the past painful experiences have not been resolved, and the disaster in Hebei-East has come again. This is truly a major national crisis. All of our people should unanimously support national rights and cannot sell out in the slightest. Our association has read the clear orders of your government and the Executive Yuan regarding the recent Hebei-East autonomy issue, and has taken emergency steps. However, the handling of the incident should be quick and not slow. A slight hesitation may lead to further complications. Moreover, Hebei-East is the gateway to North China, and its market is especially important for the production life of the southeastern provinces. If the territory is divided, not only will the situation in the southeast be affected, but also national taxes and domestic economy will be affected. Past facts can be taken as a warning. We hereby request that your government and the Executive Yuan immediately order He, the Chief of Office, to take office quickly, and also issue clear orders to the local generals to be responsible for suppressing the rebels, stabilizing the overall situation, and securing the territory. We telegraph urgently, and respectfully ask for your consideration. The Chinese General Federation of Industry gratefully thanks you.

Telegraph to the Generals: (1) The City Federation telegraphed to the Generals of North China, saying: Commander Song of the Beiping Garrison, Chairman of Hebei Province, Chairman Han of Shandong Province, Mayor Cheng of Tianjin, [all recipients] Jian, Yin Rugeng organized the Hebei-East Autonomous Anti-Communist Committee in Tongzhou on [a certain day], declaring independence, betraying the country, and destroying the integrity of our territory. At this time of crisis, you have the responsibility to protect the border. We urge you to uphold justice, quickly send elite troops, and issue clear orders to suppress, correct the people's views, and defend the nation forever. We telegraph and report, and wait for your instructions, (2) The Chinese General Federation of Industry telegraphed: Commander Song of the Beiping Garrison Headquarters, Chairman Shang of the Baoding Provincial Government, Chairman Han of the Jinan Provincial Government, according to reports, Hebei-East has declared autonomy and seceded from the central government. The people of the whole country are deeply indignant at this insane and absurd action. You are loyal and patriotic, and we have long admired you. We hope that you will decisively eliminate the rebels, so as to uphold the national law and stabilize the country. We are eager to await your orders. The Chinese General Federation of Industry gratefully thanks you.

Heavy Snow in Zhengzhou Yesterday, Eurasia Aircraft Delayed in Xi'an, Blindly Took Off from Chengdu in the Morning, Encountered Clouds on the Way and Avoided Danger 77

According to Huadong She, the second giant aircraft of the Eurasia Airlines Junkers 52 type, No. 52, was scheduled to travel eastward yesterday (Wednesday), but the weather in Shaanxi and Sichuan changed drastically yesterday. However, in order to ensure the accuracy of the schedule, Eurasia Airlines still took off as usual. It took off from Chengdu at 8 am at the risk of its flight, but unexpectedly, at about 10 am, it encountered dark clouds and the weather was extremely dull in the Qinling Mountains, where Chengdu and Xi'an meet. The aircraft flew blindly in the clouds and continued to move forward. Finally, at 10:30 am, it emerged from the clouds and avoided danger, and landed safely in Xi'an at 11 am. The aircraft originally planned to fly to Shanghai again, but because of the heavy snow in the Zhengzhou area, it stayed in Shaanxi and waited for the weather to improve today before returning to Shanghai. A spokesman for the company told a reporter from Huadong She yesterday that the aircraft telegraphed the company in Shanghai, saying that during the flight this morning (ie yesterday morning), it was blocked by dense clouds at all times. Fortunately, the aircraft was equipped with blind flight instruments, so it was able to ascend upwards, enter the clouds directly, and continue to move forward in the absence of any targets, so it could safely fly to its destination in Xi'an over the high mountains covered by clouds. This is said to be the first successful adventure of Chinese civil aviation.

Appropriating Funds to Promote Acceptance Bills, Banks Studying Methods, Qian Industry Advocating Prior Handling of Type A, Central Bank Agreeing to Rediscount 78

The Shanghai Industry and Commerce Loan Review Committee decided to allocate 3 million yuan from the credit small loan item as a fund for the acceptance and discount of industrial and commercial bills, and sent letters to the bank and Qian industry associations to solicit opinions. The Qian industry association has now approved the principle and will first handle Type A, that is, raw materials and goods are stored in warehouses. Those that have been identified as needed and valuable in the market can fill out bank acceptance bills according to the prescribed discount, and the trustee bank or firm will accept them. Type B will be postponed, that is, commercial acceptance bills obtained from the sale of goods can be applied for discount to the trustee bank or firm. If the persons related to the above bills are found to have considerable assets, they can be exempted from providing guarantees. The Banking Association has set up a small committee to study the matter. A reporter from Xin Sheng She learned from the banking industry yesterday that the members of the small committee, such as Luo Qinghua, have begun to study the matter. After a decision is made, they will report to the association. As for the rediscount case, the Central Bank has agreed to handle it and is now preparing the method by the Business Bureau.

Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau to Hold Simple Life Insurance, To Be Launched in Shanghai and Nanjing on the Second of Next Month, Hankou Arrangement Not Yet Completed, To Be Launched on the Tenth 80

The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau will launch simple life insurance and has decided to conduct trial operations in Nanjing, Shanghai, and Hankou starting next month. The insurance regulations, etc., have been submitted to the Ministry for approval, and the Ministry has also recruited staff to specialize in their duties. After the results of the examination are announced, they will be assigned to serve in various places. The following is a record of the various situations.

Internal Organization The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau will launch simple life insurance. Its insurance law was submitted to the Executive Yuan by the Ministry of Communications and approved by the Legislative Yuan for promulgation. Recently, the Ministry ordered the Bureau to prepare for it. An insurance office was established, and its internal organization is divided into five groups, responsible for general affairs, business, accounting, statistics, contract, and other matters. The personnel have been transferred and appointed by the Bureau. All insurance regulations and application rules have also been formulated by the Bureau and submitted to the Ministry for approval. They have now been printed.

Scheduled Trial Operation The insurance business will be temporarily launched in Nanjing, Shanghai, and Hankou. Shanghai and Nanjing will be launched on December 2nd, and Hankou will be launched on the 10th of the same month due to the unfinished arrangements. The Bureau has now issued invitations, saying, "Our Bureau has scheduled to launch simple life insurance business on December 2nd. Recruiting Staff The Ministry of Communications specially recruited staff in Nanjing to specialize in their duties for the purpose of launching life insurance. The written examination has now been completed and the examination papers are being graded. After the list of those admitted is announced, an oral examination will be held. The staff in the three places are currently temporarily transferred from various bureaus. After the staff admitted are announced, they will be assigned to serve in various places. It is also heard that the organizational law of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau is being drafted by the Ministry after it was merged into the General Post Office. There is no change in the various offices established, but the various groups established under the offices will be changed to sections.

Eurasia Aviation Corporation Sends Personnel to Study in Germany; Second Group of Seven to Depart Early Next Month; Li Jing Discusses the Cultivation of Talent 82

Eurasia Aviation Corporation has consistently dispatched personnel to various countries over the years to study aviation and mechanical techniques. It is learned that this year's group includes He Shou-rong, Lin Qing-dai, Rong Guan-dui, Chen Feng-qi, Zhang Yan-tang, Yang Bao-fan, and Feng Shi-jing, a total of seven individuals. Their passports have all been processed, and they will depart early next month. A reporter from the Central News Agency, upon learning of this, visited Mr. Li Jing-cong, the company's general manager, yesterday. According to Mr. Li (hereinafter Li's remarks), although civil aviation in our country has made considerable progress in recent years, the technical aspects still require assistance from foreign personnel. While these foreign personnel have the responsibility of teaching domestic technicians, they often prefer to use apprentices because of their familiarity with the techniques, ease of management, and lack of effort required. Therefore, they often advocate for hiring craftsmen as a principle. I believe that while hiring craftsmen is indeed useful, most have not received formal education. To expect them to contribute to the development of the national aviation industry or shoulder responsibility in the future based on their experience is unlikely. Therefore, since becoming the general manager of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, I have strived to overcome the prejudice of foreign personnel and, in addition to craftsmen, have diligently worked to cultivate advanced domestic technicians both at home and abroad. For the past three years, we have consistently trained personnel based on this policy. Those recruited are graduates of domestic and foreign mechanical schools, high schools, or aviation academies. Currently, there are over forty successfully trained mechanics serving at various stations along the line, as well as at the two repair factories in Beiping Nanyuan and Shanghai Longhua. There are also four assigned to aircraft for flight duties and six serving as on-board mechanics and communications personnel, all of whom have received blind flight training. These mechanics and flight personnel are technically no less skilled than foreign flight and mechanical personnel. As for sending them abroad for further study, it is aimed at pursuing deeper knowledge to catch up quickly. This is because our country's current equipment, in all aspects, is still far behind others. Eurasia Aviation Corporation sent five people to study in Germany the autumn before last, including Zhou Zhao-lin, Chen Zhao-wei, Fang Wen-ji, Fan Jing-lan, and Hu Hui-jian. Most of them have successfully completed their studies and will soon be ordered to return home for employment. This is the second group being sent, including Feng Shi-jing, Chen Feng-qi, He Shou-rong, Rong Guan-dui, Lin Qing-dai, Zhang Yan-tang, and Yang Bao-fan, a total of seven individuals. They have all received one to three years of training at Eurasia Aviation Corporation. Not only is their technical skill reliable, but their character is also excellent. The physical condition of He Shou-rong, Chen Feng-qi, Lin Qing-dai, and Rong Guan-dui, who are studying flight, has been examined by the German doctor Knoll and deemed satisfactory and qualified. The study period is approximately two to three years. Zhang Yan-tang, Feng Shi-jing, and Yang Bao-fan are going to study mechanics or materials management, for a period of approximately one year or more. The practice of sending personnel abroad for study will continue annually to ensure the continuous training of domestic flight and mechanical personnel, preventing any interruption or a feeling of insufficient supply in the future. Eurasia Aviation Corporation has also sent letters to various industrial universities, requesting them to recommend graduates of engineering departments with excellent academic records, character, and integrity for trial employment. The best candidates will be selected for thorough training. In the future, if Chinese individuals or companies wish to establish domestic aviation routes, I am very willing to select several individuals from among the already trained domestic flight and mechanical personnel who are knowledgeable, experienced, and persevering, and recommend them for their service, to jointly develop the aviation industry. As for the members of this group being sent, their luggage and passports have been processed. I will fly to Beijing this afternoon to accompany them to meet with Minister Zhu and Vice Ministers Yu and Zhang of the Ministry of Transportation, to personally request instructions before departing early next month.

Telegraph Bureau; Smooth Telephone Telegraph Service; Over Seven Hundred Telegrams Sent in the Last Five Days; Trial Operation Increases Business by Over One-Fifth 83

The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, recognizing that in the past, after 6:00 PM, there were only two places in the city to send telegrams: the bureau's main office and the radio receiving station on Minguo Road. Given the vast area of the city, having only two locations to send telegrams caused inconvenience for those who lived far from these locations and needed to send urgent telegrams. Therefore, starting on the evening of the 22nd, a method of sending telegrams by telephone was implemented on a trial basis for a period of three months. As of yesterday (the 26th), the trial had been in effect for five days. According to Mr. Xu Bao-hua of the bureau, speaking to a reporter from the New Sound News Agency yesterday morning, the bureau's purpose in trying this method was to reduce the difficulty and obstacles for citizens sending telegrams. The method of sending telegrams by telephone is as follows: citizens with telephones at home who need to send a telegram after 6:00 PM can immediately notify the bureau's main office by telephone (telephone number 13082). They can report the desired message over the phone, and the bureau's staff will immediately record it. They will then call back to confirm with the sender that the message is correct and send it immediately, quickly and efficiently. As for the telegraph fee, the bureau's staff will calculate it based on the number of words and issue a receipt, sending someone to the sender's home the next morning to collect the fee, saving trouble and avoiding the inconvenience of sending someone to collect the fee at night. Since the implementation on the evening of the 22nd, over seven hundred telegrams have been sent as of yesterday, which is more enthusiastic than expected. Therefore, it is predicted that after a month of trial operation, business will increase by more than one-fifth. After three months of trial operation, there will be even better results, and the bureau will officially adopt this method. The telephone telegraph service will be available from 6:00 PM to 7:00 AM every night, and all day on Sundays.

Central Agricultural Experiment Station Publishes This Year's Flood and Drought Losses in Various Provinces 85

In view of the severe disasters in various provinces this year, the Central Agricultural Experiment Station drafted a survey form in September and distributed it to over six thousand agricultural reporters nationwide for investigation and reporting. The investigation has now been completed, covering 730 counties in thirteen provinces, including Shaanxi, Shanxi, Hebei, Shandong, Jiangsu, Anhui, Henan, Hubei, Hunan, Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Guangdong. 216 counties reported floods, and 279 reported droughts. The total amount of grain loss is recorded as follows:

Flood Losses: The total affected area is 35,002,000 mu, and the total grain loss is 55,318,000 dan, including 22,445,000 dan of rice, 7,187,000 dan of sorghum, 7,738,000 dan of millet, 945,000 dan of broomcorn millet, 6,460,000 dan of corn, and 10,543,000 dan of soybeans. The most severe flood losses this year were in Hubei Province, with 14,451,000 dan of grain lost, Shandong Province, with 12,834,000 dan of grain lost, Henan Province, with 7,439,000 dan of grain lost, and Hebei Province, with 6,382,000 dan of grain lost.

Drought Losses: The total affected area is 58,618,000 mu, and the total grain loss is 77,027,000 dan, including 23,969,000 dan of rice, 8,358,000 dan of sorghum, 10,057,000 dan of millet, 1,668,000 dan of broomcorn millet, 7,753,000 dan of corn, and 25,222,000 dan of soybeans. The most severe drought losses this year were in Anhui Province, with 19,977,000 dan of grain lost, Shandong Province, with 15,382,000 dan of grain lost, Hebei Province, with 11,716,000 dan of grain lost, Jiangsu Province, with 10,825,000 dan of grain lost, and Henan Province, with 9,026,000 dan of grain lost.

Total Losses: The total amount of grain loss from the above flood and drought disasters is 132,345,000 dan. If each dan of grain is priced at three yuan, the loss of crops due to flood and drought disasters this year is approximately 400 million yuan.

(5) The establishment of armyworm control subcommittees in various districts will be temporarily postponed. (6) The armyworm control movement subcommittee's publicity week will be held after Arbor Day in the 25th year of the Republic. (7) Purchase moth-luring lamps and request the Central Propaganda Committee to screen armyworm control films, and reprint 3,000 armyworm control picture posters and 300 copies of the "Armyworm Control Primer." (8) It was found that the countryside of this county mostly plants early rice, and the rice roots have now been plowed. The first phase of armyworm control work cannot be started and should be postponed to the second phase.

Freight Train on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Derailed at Hushu Pass Last Night; Shanghai-Bound Express Train from Beijing Delayed 94

Freight train No. 503, traveling from Beijing to Shanghai on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, derailed two wheels of the locomotive at the rear of engine B-47 and six wheels of the coal and water car as it passed through the east fork of the Hushu Pass station at approximately 9:00 PM yesterday. This blocked both the up and down lines. The stationmaster immediately sent a telegram for assistance. Upon receiving the news, the railway bureau immediately dispatched senior officials from the vehicle, engineering, and machinery departments, along with workers, on a rescue train to the scene of the accident at approximately 11:00 PM. They worked to repair the damage. A rescue train from Changzhou also went to assist in the repairs, which were still not completed as of 1:00 AM this morning. The third special express train from Beijing to Shanghai, which departed at 5:00 PM yesterday and was scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at 11:30 PM last night, was blocked at Hushu Station and could not proceed. It is expected to arrive in Shanghai around dawn this morning.

Ministry of Transportation Accommodates Banks and Money Exchanges in Sending Telegrams; Code Numbers Can Be Added to the Beginning and End of Telegrams 95

The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation received a letter from the Directorate General of Telegraphs, which reads: I am writing to inform you that Article 54(b) of the Domestic Telegraph Business Regulations stipulates that banks and money exchanges may add a code number and an Arabic numeral indicating the date and number of the telegram to the end or beginning of the telegram text. It has been found that commercial firms also add the above code number and numeral to Chinese plain language telegrams sent for remittance purposes. It should be permitted to adopt the same practice and charge according to the Chinese plain language rate to show accommodation. Furthermore, the above measures should be drafted by each bureau as a press release and sent to the local newspapers for widespread publicity. Please check and instruct all affiliated bureaus and offices to comply accordingly. To the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau.

Loading and Unloading Workers at the Two Railway North Freight Stations; Managed by the Railway Administration; Originally Handled by the Loading and Unloading Workers Cooperative, Resulting in Repeated Disputes; Now Managed by the Traffic Department, Resulting in Increased Wages for the Workers 97

The loading and unloading work at the North Freight Station on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway was originally handled by the North Loading and Unloading Workers Cooperative. However, due to workers competing for work and other reasons, there were repeated disturbances and occasional械鬥incidents, which greatly affected transportation and security. In order to improve work efficiency and enhance worker welfare, the Ministry of Railways specifically ordered the railway to be directly managed by the Traffic Department, which has been implemented since the 16th of last month. It is heard that since the railway's Traffic Department took over the operation, it has conducted worker registration, assigned administrators, and strictly formulated management regulations, and the operation has been very smooth. It has also been determined that all loading and unloading fees, except for 10% to be set aside as a public welfare fund for worker welfare and incentives, will be distributed equally to the workers. The salaries of the administrators are also paid by the railway. According to investigations, the half-month salary for October has been issued by the department, with each person receiving 21 yuan and 98 fen. It is estimated that each person can earn around 50 yuan per month, which is a significant increase from the previous 10 yuan per month. The workers are all satisfied.

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Music Committee held a meeting on the 20th of this month. However, he did not object to the conductor's proposal. Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry: Proposal to Discuss Dyeing Prices at Meeting 100

The Shanghai Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Association has recently been affected by the continuous increase in the price of dyes, exceeding 25%. Dyes are the main raw material for the dyeing industry. Recently, the dye industry has adopted cash transactions, and prices have risen without available goods, hindering the source of supply and causing panic. The standard dyeing price has always been determined based on the rise and fall of dye prices. Usually, dyeing prices are settled with silk merchants. However, some brokers, in order to secure business, accommodate the situation and slightly deviate from the dyeing price agreed upon by the competent authorities. The dyeing industry requires dyes, coal, and technicians, resulting in high costs. As a result, the dyeing price is often insufficient to cover the material costs and expenses. Many companies have suffered losses and gone bankrupt as a result. Even those with strong capital are struggling in this unfavorable economic situation, feeling exhausted. Now that the government has implemented the legal tender policy, the economy has changed, and various industries are raising prices to adapt to the economic environment and make up for losses. The association once convened a meeting to discuss pricing plans and assigned personnel to negotiate. The sub-committee has now made three recommendations: (1) "The dyeing price standard should be increased by 25% based on the original dyeing price settled with the silk merchants by each industry, and all should comply." (2) "The implementation measures for the proposed price increase should be created in the form of a price list and reported to the competent authorities for record. If any industry intentionally raises prices or secretly lowers the price standard, once the facts are verified, severe punishment should be requested from the association in accordance with Municipal Government Orders No. 161 and 162." (3) "The length of silk and satin should be restricted. The measurement should be based on the municipal foot of the metric system, and each piece should not exceed fifty feet. If the length exceeds the limit, the dyeing price should be calculated proportionally per foot to facilitate work and improve the quality of dyeing." It is reported that the aforementioned recommendations will be presented for discussion at the general meeting today.

Tianchan Stage Managed by Gu Zhuxuan Suddenly Suspended Performances: The Reason is the Small Commission Payment Issue, Currently Being Mediated, Expected to Resume Performances 101

According to Huadong News Agency, Tianchan Stage, managed by Gu Zhuxuan, suddenly suspended performances for the past two days. The main reason is a dispute over small commission payments. Mediation is currently underway, and performances are expected to resume within days. The general audience, unaware of the reason, still numbered in the thousands yesterday, and the reporter has investigated the details as follows:

Ten Years of History Since Opening: Tianchan Stage is located at the corner of Yunnan Road on the Fourth Avenue of this port. It was founded by Gu Zhuxuan, who was recently involved in the case of the assassination of Tang Jiapeng, the manager of the Great World. It has been open for nearly ten years. Business was quite dull before. The January 28th Incident caused it to suspend performances for two months. After resuming performances, business flourished, especially when the Fu Liancheng Troupe visited Shanghai. This summer, famous actors such as Zhao Ruquan, Bai Yukun, Bu Yunfang, Zhao Junyu, Yang Dingnong, Liu Kunrong, and Wang Fuying were hired, and the entire Legend of Jigong was newly arranged. Business became increasingly prosperous, with almost every day sold out.

Gu's Case Occurred, Lack of Funds: Two months ago, Gu was arrested by the French police for his involvement in the assassination of Tang Jiapeng. After the case occurred, the theater's finances became strained. Although efforts were made to tighten expenses, including ceasing advertising in newspapers and other expenses on the 11th of this month, it was still difficult to manage. As a result, a portion of the small commission payments to the backstage staff were inevitably delayed. The suspension of performances occurred on the evening before last (the 26th) due to this dispute.

Currently Mediating, Expected to Resume: According to a person from the theater, the management promised to mediate the small commission payment issue at 5:00 PM the evening before last. However, negotiations failed, so some actors refused to perform. Mediation is continuing, and performances are expected to resume within days. As for the large commission payments to Zhao Ruquan and others, there is no problem. After the theater's sudden suspension of performances, the general audience, unaware of the truth, still went to see the show yesterday, only to find that it had been suspended, and all shouted that they had been cheated.

Salt Fan Special Issue: First Prize-Winning Essay Announced, Winner: Liu Jun 103

Mr. Jing Benbai, president of the Salt Administration Magazine, launched the first prize-winning essay contest for the Salt Fan Special Issue last November. The results have now been reviewed by integrity experts. Although more than ten people wrote about Topic A (A Plan and Procedure for Implementing the Salt Law), only Mr. Liu Hanlie was selected. Mr. Liu's original name is Juan, and he is a specialist in salt affairs at the Institute of Social Sciences of the Academia Sinica. The plan he proposed is thorough and precise, excelling not only in writing. Dr. Zuo Shuzhen, a salt law expert, commented that it was carefully written based on the new law, planning everything in an orderly manner, showing enthusiasm for salt affairs and research. He added that this essay was the best submission for this topic. Mr. Chen Changheng, a member of the Legislative Yuan and the original drafter of the Salt Law, commented that the essay had a full understanding of the legislative spirit and a detailed design of the implementation procedure, and was a masterpiece. Mr. Jing Benbai commented that the design was thorough and feasible. He quoted Mencius's words to Duke Wen of Teng: "If a king arises, he will surely take it as a model." If the salt law is not implemented, then so be it. If it is to be implemented, then it must be modeled after this. The author has only studied salt affairs for three years, yet his progress is so great. The younger generation is formidable, and there are successors. There is hope for reform. The original first prize of 300 yuan will be awarded to Mr. Liu, and the second prize will be added to the award to Mr. Liu, for a total of 500 yuan. The original manuscript has over 30,000 words. In addition to being published in the Salt Fan Special Issue, it will also be sent to major newspapers for publication. The essay rules have been seen in this newspaper's advertisement.

A Novel Scam Case: Reprinting the Bottom Page of Book Plates to Sell at High Prices 104

Hu Fuchu, who claimed to be an employee of the Labor Department of the Ministry of Industry, with a thin face, tall stature, short beard, and wearing a Western suit, came to the Zhen Dan University Library in West Shanghai to sell the China Labor Yearbook, which was commissioned by the Ministry of Industry to be sold by the Zhengzhong Book Company, priced at five yuan per copy. The school, seeing the signatures of Jiaotong University and other institutions on his sales book, purchased a copy without suspicion, calculating at 80% of the listed price, paying four yuan. Mr. Hu wrote a receipt on his business card. Unexpectedly, after checking the Zhengzhong Book Company's catalog, the hardcover edition was only sold for three yuan and fifty cents. After closer inspection, it was found that the copyright page had been torn off and the price had been reprinted, revealing the deception. Therefore, the school sent a letter to the Shanghai Distribution Office of Zhengzhong Book Company, reporting the deception. The bureau immediately reported to the Nanjing General Bureau, requesting an investigation from the Ministry of Industry nearby and instructions on how to handle the situation. The bureau has now received a reply from the Labor Department of the Ministry of Industry, stating, "We have received your letter and understand the situation. We have no such person as Hu Fuchu in our department. It is obviously an impersonation. In addition to secretly investigating through other means, please also inform Zhen Dan University and other libraries that if this situation is discovered again, please immediately detain the person and send them to the competent authorities for investigation. We are responding to your inquiry." The bureau, believing that there was no Mr. Hu in the Ministry of Industry, sent a letter to Zhen Dan University and issued a statement in the newspaper, and is conducting a thorough investigation to warn against wrongdoing.
