High Court Third Branch Under Heavy Security: Gu Zhuxuan's Appeal Case Heard, Judge Ordered Gu to State Himself Yesterday, Gu Said He Was Completely Falsely Accused, Zhao Guangfu's Testimony Was Evasive, Much of What He Said Was Unrelated to the Case, Zhang Tinggui Was Called to Testify, Describing the Events Before and After the Shooting of Tang Jiapeng 105

Gu Zhuxuan, the owner of the Tianchan Stage from Yancheng, was implicated in the assassination of Tang Jiapeng, the manager of the Great World. After being reported and arrested by the convicted Zhao Guangfu for incitement, he appealed to the High Court Third Branch against the fifteen-year prison sentence imposed by the Second Special District Court. The details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday was the date of the hearing. The High Court also took precautions, as it considered the case to be serious, and the security was as strict as before at the Second Special District Court. After 12 o'clock, the Second Special District Court ordered the eastern side door to be closed and entry and exit through the main entrance. The French police also dispatched a reserve team of Chinese police officers to distribute around the court to guard and protect, and dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to maintain order together with the French police.

Gu's relatives and friends who came to court to listen did not decrease due to the cloudy and rainy weather. Those who arrived early received tickets to enter the first courtroom and sat quietly for the trial. Those who arrived late could not enter without tickets and had to wait outside for news. Gu Zhuxuan was still detained in the Guangci Hospital due to illness. The bailiff went to the hospital with the High Court Third Branch's warrant and brought Gu to the criminal court one, where the judge, accompanied by the clerk Wu Jiayu, together with the prosecutor Dong Qiming, opened a collegiate panel for trial. The Police Affairs Office was represented in court by lawyer Yao Zhaodi. The legal advisor of the Municipal Council

Mr. Jiatang (transliteration) and his secretary Mr. Li Jiaer (transliteration) also attended to listen. After the court opened, Gu arrived. Gu wore a blue silk-lined velvet robe, with short stubble on his upper lip. Standing before the case, the judge first asked his age, place of origin, occupation, and address. Then, the judge stated that he had been sentenced to fifteen years in prison and had filed an appeal. He asked him to state the reasons for his appeal. Gu replied, "I have a lawyer, please let the lawyer speak for me." The judge said, "You can state it yourself, you don't need a lawyer to speak for you." Gu immediately stated his reasons, saying, "I was really

completely falsely accused. The most obvious thing is, how can someone owe money for two or three years? I really don't know the facts. Moreover, Tang Jiapeng and I are the best of friends, and we are also fellow apprentices. I have never committed a crime in Shanghai in the past thirty or forty years. This time, I have been falsely accused, and I ask the court to seek justice. Zhao Guangfu wanted to blackmail me, the facts are all there." The judge asked, "Did you know Tang Jiapeng?" Gu replied, "He was my best friend. We often met at Huang's house. We don't share wealth or work together, so how can there be resentment?" The judge asked, "What relationship does Tang Jiapeng have with your Tianchan Stage?" Gu replied, "No relationship. I run the Tianchan Stage, and he is the manager of the Great World.

We have no grudges. "The judge asked, "Do you know Zhao Guangfu and Zhang Xiaosizi (i.e., Zhang Tinggui)?" Gu replied, "I don't know them." The judge asked, "Do you know Wang Xinggao?" Gu replied, "He is a debt collector. I often see him in the newspapers." The judge asked, "Do you have a mentor-student relationship with Wang Xinggao?" Gu replied, "No relationship. We are just from the same village." The judge asked, "According to you, you don't even know the names of Zhao and Zhang?" Gu replied, "Yes. I heard in court that they said they were rickshaw pullers." The judge asked, "The three letters presented, one from Zhao Guangfu to you, and two from Xue Zhenyi to you, when did you receive Zhao's letter?" Gu replied, "I received it at home, and it was found later." The judge asked, "Do you know what the letter said?" Gu replied, "At that time, I was sick, and my family told me that

he wanted to bite me and would not bite unless I gave him money." The judge asked, "What did Xue's letter say? You should know that, right?" Gu replied, "My family also received it. I was sick and confused. Xue also wrote a letter to Zheng Jiansan, and Zheng told me that you have this matter, then you should think of a way, otherwise you don't need to pay attention to him." The judge asked, "Who is Zheng?" Gu replied, "He is my relative, he used to be a messenger, and he worked in the party headquarters. He is also a businessman now." The judge asked, "Is Wang Xing really your apprentice?" Gu replied, "There is no such thing." The judge asked, "What is the relationship between Wang, Zhao, Zhang, etc.?" Gu replied, "I don't know." The judge asked, "Is the Da Jiangnan Hotel yours? When did it open?" Gu replied, "I opened it before the January 28th Incident. I don't often go there." The judge asked,

"Have you been to the Asia Hotel?" Gu replied, "This is a small hotel. I have never been there." The judge asked, "Have you been to the Asia Hotel for other matters in the past year?" Gu replied, "I have never been there. The accountant and the receptionist have testified before." The judge asked, "How did you get to know Xue Zhenyi?" Gu replied, "He is the head of the Red Cross rescue team. I am a director in the Red Cross. During the January 28th Incident, I ran a refugee camp and met him." The judge asked, "Why did Xue call you teacher?" Gu replied, "That was his polite way of addressing me." After questioning to this point, when Zhao Guangfu was ordered to be brought up, Gu Zhuxuan's defense lawyer Xue Dubi stated to the court that the appellant was not fully recovered from his illness and was not clear-minded. He was afraid that he would not be able to stand for a long time, and his body would not be able to support it. He requested the court to allow

him to be seated while waiting for questioning. The court approved, and a chair was given. However, it was ordered that he must stand up when giving testimony. Gu agreed and sat down. Then Zhao Guangfu was brought to the case. The judge first asked his age, place of origin, occupation, and address. Then, the judge told Zhao that today he was being questioned about the matter of him reporting Gu Zhuxuan, and he should tell the truth and not lie. He was ordered to state the beginning and end of the Tang case. Zhao stood still and did not speak. After the court urged him, Zhao spoke from the section of being arrested by the Putuo Road police station on June 24th, all of which were unrelated to the Tang case. After the court ordered him to state the events before and after the killing of Tang, not to talk about matters outside the case, Zhao still stammered. Then, the court reviewed the case file from the previous case and questioned Zhao. Zhao's testimony was generally the same as in the previous case, but when he testified, he

stammered or feigned a dull state. After the court questioned Zhao in detail, Gu's defense lawyer Shan Yuhua rose and said that last time he requested to review the files, he only reviewed the files of this case, and the files of previous cases were not reviewed. In addition to the ten points of reasons raised by the appellant, there are a few more points. He requested a scheduled file review to supplement the reasons. He said that he had another court hearing at the moment, and asked to be allowed to leave the court first. The court stated that he could review the files except for Wednesday, Saturday afternoons. If the lawyer had another case, he could leave first. Lawyer Shan left first. Later, the court ordered Zhang Tinggui (i.e., Xiaosizi) to be brought to the case. After asking his age and origin, the judge informed him that he

should tell the truth and ordered him to take an oath before ordering him to state the situation before and after the killing of Tang. Zhang testified that there were four people who killed Tang Jiapeng, namely Gu Dunyang, Zhou Qifu, Zhao Guangfu, and me. First, on June 12, I met Wang Jinkui at the intersection of Chang'an Road and Hengfeng Road in Zhabei. I asked him to find me a job. He said that he would ask Zhou Qifu to call me to the Asia Hotel tomorrow. I asked him what it was about. He said that he wanted to beat to death an enemy. On the next day, June 13, Zhou Qifu came to call me to the Asia Hotel. There were six or seven people in the room. He told me to wait outside. I did not know Gu Zhuxuan at first. Later, I saw Gu take out two pistols and give them to Wang Jinkui, and said that he entrusted this matter to him (referring to Wang Jinkui), and then went out. Wang told me that the one who was just now was the fourth boss, Gu. Then Gu Dunyang, Zhou Qifu, Wang Jinkui, and I went to Luzon Road

in front of Tang's house to take a look, and then went home. Before leaving, Wang told me that I must come. On June 16, I first waited at the Tiger Stove on Longmen Road. At 11:00 PM, Zhao Guangfu came. I did not know Zhao. Wang said to call Zhao and Gu Dunyang to beat Tang Xiapeng. Sun Er pulled a rickshaw to deliver the pistol. Nothing happened that night. The next evening, we met at the original place and waited under the big clock opposite the Great World. Zhou Qifu asked me to look at the rickshaw. He walked over, and then I heard gunshots. Zhou came back and told me to go back, and said that if the person died tomorrow, go to the Baker Road teahouse in the morning to get money. The next day, Zhou brought me to the Baker Road teahouse. Wang Jinkui told me that the fourth boss, Gu, was

in financial difficulty, and first gave me sixty yuan, and gave Zhou Qifu two hundred and ninety yuan to distribute to others, and told Zhou to take back the gun. Wang also told me to go back to the countryside to avoid the limelight, and I could still get money when I came to Shanghai. I went back to the countryside. On August 11, I set off for Shanghai again. I arrived in Shanghai on the 13th and lived in Chadaijiao. In September, I met Wang Jinkui, who asked me to go to the Tiger Stove on Haifang Road the next day to give me money. When I arrived at the Tiger Stove, I was arrested as soon as I washed my face. I said that Gu Si had told people to kill Tang Jiapeng. Later, I was sentenced to twenty years. I did not want to appeal. I planned to sue Gu Si. Xue Zhenyi persuaded me not to sue, saying that he was

Gu's apprentice, and he asked Gu to hire a lawyer to appeal for me. Because I did not have money to buy a complaint, the prisoner Liu Yimin in the detention center bought it for me. I did not know that Zhao Guangfu had accused Gu Zhuxuan. When I was taken to the police station, I was asked to identify Gu Zhuxuan, and I knew that it was Zhao who reported him. When Gu was in the Asia Hotel, he said that he would give ten thousand yuan. Gu did not speak to me in the Asia Hotel. Wang Jinkui told me. There is such a person as Wang Jinkui, who is shorter than me. I have no resentment against Gu, why should I bite him? The judge asked Gu Zhuxuan, is Zhang's words correct? Gu replied, "Completely wrong. I have never been to the Asia Hotel once. Zhao and Zhang are accomplices and have conspired. If Zhang said that he had revealed my name before, how could it be that I was

not arrested at that time?" The judge ordered Xue Zhenji to be brought to the case. According to his testimony, he did not know about Zhao Guangfu's matter before. When Zhao wanted to accuse Gu of instigating murder, he asked me to help and asked me to write a letter to mediate, wanting to get some money. Zhao looked at the Dongfang Magazine and saw Gu's photo and recognized him. I wrote two letters, and Gu did not reply. On July 3, Zhao told me that he could get the money, and he would split it 30/70. When he said this, the prisoner Zhang Shuchuan heard it. I did not express my opinion. In August, Zhao asked the prisoner Zhang Chenliang to bring me a note. I

still did not express whether I agreed. Zhao also asked Liu Yimin and Wu Shaoting to come and say to me, and I did not agree. Zhao meant to ask me to help him. I have no relationship with Gu. However, when I was the head of the rescue team, Gu was a director and took good care of us, so I wrote a letter and called him teacher. I did not say to Zhao in the detention center that I would hire a lawyer to appeal for him. Wang Xinggao was also brought to the case. He testified that I do not have the name Wang Jinkui. If this name is found, I can be shot. I have no teacher-student relationship with Gu. However, Gu is the chairman of the village association. I saw him once after the village association built a new house at a speech. I have no dealings with Gu. I originally lived at No. 4 Quanlefang, Hengfeng Road, and

The eldest son is twenty-one years old this year and has now gone to Nanjing to become a monk. However, my parents are dead. After I was arrested, I hired a lawyer, and my family pawned all my clothes. How could I have money to give Zhao Fusi four hundred yuan and one thousand yuan? When Tang Jiapeng was killed, I was in Hankou, etc. Zhao Guangfu was also brought to the case. The question was, did Wang Xinggao invite you to kill Tang Jiapeng? Italian Rayon Worth 1.5 Million Yuan Shipped to Japan 106

The most exported Italian goods to China are rayon, with a huge sales market. The price of silk has soared this year, and the price of Italian rayon has also increased accordingly, with each piece selling for more than 400 yuan. The import tariff is very high. Therefore, after the goods are shipped to Shanghai, they are stored in the Jianghai Customs warehouse. Each piece is unloaded and taxed one piece at a time. If it is not sold, the tariff is not paid. Recently, a total of 3,745 pieces of Italian rayon stored in the customs warehouse in Shanghai, weighing 430 tons, worth 1.5 million yuan, have been piled up for a long time because no one buys them. Due to the excessive losses suffered by Italian merchants and the severe shortage of sales markets in Shanghai, it has been decided to take them out of the customs warehouse and load them onto the Italian ship Tenges for sale in Japan.

All Branches Managed by Chinese Managers of the International Savings Society to be Closed: The Society Issued a Notice Yesterday, to be Implemented in July Next Year 107

In order to comply with our country's laws, the International Savings Society issued a notice to all depositors, deciding to close all branches managed by Chinese managers from July 1 next year. The notice is recorded below: The Society is a French company, founded in China in 1912, issuing prize-winning savings certificates and drawing prizes monthly, which has been recognized by the Chinese government. The new Chinese Criminal Law has been implemented on July 1, 1935. Although the law cannot be applied to the Society, a French company, the board of directors of the Society is deeply concerned that managers and promoters in various regions will be affected by the law. Therefore, it has decided to close all branches managed by Chinese managers from July 1, 1936. The Shanghai head office and the Guangzhou (Shamian), Hankou, Beiping, Tianjin, and Qingdao branches will continue to operate as usual. Depositors are requested to contact the above-mentioned head and branch offices to handle all society affairs. The prize draw of the Society will continue to be held at the Shanghai head office on the 15th of each month. If the 15th is a holiday, it will be held on the next day. Sincerely, the Head Office of the International Savings Society.

Far East Giant Bell: Invitation for Tenders to Cast - Bell Body Made of Copper, Weighing 18,000 Catties - Grand Opening Ceremony of Another Large Bell Tower in Zhabei 108

Datong News Agency reports that six organizations in this city – the Buddhist Laymen's Forest, the Buddhist Studies Bureau, the Buddhist Pure Land Society, the Chinese Buddhist Association, the Jiuhua Buddhist Association, and the Shanghai Buddhist Association – have jointly initiated the casting of a giant bronze bell weighing 18,000 catties. It will be named "Netherworld" and will eventually be placed on Mount Jiuhua. As for funding, the following amounts have already been raised: the Buddhist Laymen's Forest: 10,600 yuan; the Buddhist Studies Bureau: 9,500 yuan; the Buddhist Pure Land Society: 1,907 yuan; the Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Buddhist Association: 173 yuan, totaling 22,180 yuan.

Material Research: Regarding the material of the giant bell, opinions differ due to its relation to the sound produced. Some advocate using red copper, pure copper, or a mixture of 70% copper and 30% other metals. Others suggest recasting old copper, while still others propose using a mixture of copper and iron. Therefore, public opinions were solicited last month, and after deliberation, it has been decided that using copper alloy is most suitable for producing a grand and resonant sound. Tenders are now being invited for its construction.

Site Survey: The foundation of the bell tower has been surveyed by Li Jingwei and Shen Binhan, standing committee members of the preparatory committee, at Mount Jiuhua in Anhui. A piece of land of over one mu has been selected. The land belongs to the Bai Sui (Hundred Years) Temple. The abbot of the temple has agreed to lend it permanently. Formal permanent loan agreements have been signed, exchanged, and kept by both parties. Construction can therefore commence. To ensure its solidity and resistance to wind and rain, the bell tower will be built using stone.

Another Large Bell: The Baolian Temple, located on Gonghe Xin Road, Zhongxing Road, in Zhabei, is a branch temple of the Guoen Temple in this city. The abbot, Kaisheng, previously lent a portion of vacant land to the City Buddhist Association to establish a Charity Nursery. Furthermore, he continued to renovate the interior. This summer, the construction of a four-story bell tower was completed, and a large bell weighing 3,000 catties was hung to spread a loud sound, promoting the orthodox faith in the world. The construction has now been completed, and the opening ceremony of the bell tower will be held on December 6th according to the Gregorian calendar to commemorate the occasion.

Notice from the Hotel Association: Uniform Room Rate Discounts - Fixed at 20% off Starting Next Month - All Discounted Room Rate Gifts Will Be Banned 109

The Hotel Association has decided to implement uniform room rate discounts for all hotels starting December 1st, notifying all members of the association: This notice concerns the following: According to Instruction No. 10897 from the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, all industries should determine balanced prices based on the cost and notify all members, whether they are specialized or part-time, members or non-members, must uniformly and forcibly comply. The price list and the standard of negotiation should be submitted to the bureau for record. After investigation, it is found that the current room rate discounts in the industry vary, and some even inflate the original price and then give a low discount to gain advantages, which is inappropriate and in urgent need of rectification. A general meeting of members was held at the Far East Hotel at 2:00 PM on the 25th of this month, discussing and deciding on six implementation measures for uniform room rate discounts for the industry, which are recorded as follows: (1) The uniform room rate should be discounted by 20% off the marked price as the standard discount, but the original price should not be inflated. (2) All advertisements and signs with discounts lower than the standard discount should be canceled. (3) After implementing the 20% off the marked price, similar methods such as gifts should not be used as disguised standard discounts. (4) All members and non-members should uniformly comply with these measures. (5) These measures will be incorporated into the industry regulations. If anyone deliberately violates these measures, the association may propose disciplinary measures based on the industry regulations and submit them to the Bureau of Social Affairs for approval. (6) These measures will be implemented starting December 1, 1935. All members are specially notified to comply. All preferential coupons, value coupons, prize gift coupons, etc. issued by the industry before will also be declared invalid starting December 1. In addition to reporting to the Bureau of Social Affairs for record, this notice is specially issued for general information.

South Station Switching - Locomotive - Injures Two Children - Boy Loses Toes, Girl Loses Left Arm - Parents Deeply Saddened by the Sudden Accident 110

At 11:20 AM yesterday, the No. 801 freight train from Shanghai South Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, heading to Hangzhou, arrived at Xinlonghua Station. It was waiting for the freight train from Maigen Road to Hangzhou to connect and proceed to Hangzhou. The locomotive was detached and returned to South Station. When passing Zhangjiazhai, Xizhalan, south of the S516 utility pole, two children, a boy and a girl aged three, were playing nearby. Due to the distance from the railway police and the gloomy weather, the driver Wang San could not see clearly. When the train approached, the two children did not know to avoid it and were both run over by the locomotive. The boy, Yu Sanbao, injured his left foot and had his toes crushed. The girl, Lu Genbao, had her left arm broken and was bleeding profusely. Both collapsed on the ground in pain. The driver stopped the train and reported to the South Station Chief Zhou Binwu, who dispatched police to rescue them. After bandaging at the South Station Railway Clinic, they were sent to the North Station Railway General Clinic for treatment. The girl, Lu Genbao, was in critical condition. The boy, Yu Sanbao, had his toes amputated and his life was saved. The Railway Police Department investigated and found that the boy's father, Yu Ashan, and the girl's father, Lu Yan, were both railway workers living nearby at No. 23 Jixiang Lane. Both children were only children. They were deeply saddened by the sudden accident.

Municipal Bureau of Education - Strictly Prohibits Obscene Operas - Special Meeting Held to Instruct Bang Bang Opera Performers - Today at 10:00 AM at the People's Education Hall 111

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, in view of the performances of Bai Yushuang and others at the Empire Theatre, where the singing and movements of the Bang Bang Opera performers were deemed obscure and offensive, originally intended to strictly prohibit the performances. However, in consideration of the livelihood of the performers, the Bureau has been sending members of the opera review committee to the theatre every day to strictly review the content. Up to now, the following nine operas have been approved for performance: "Velvet Note," "The Prodigal Son Returns," "Du Shiniang," "Lotus Nunnery," "Peach Blossom Nunnery," "Li Guixiang Chops Wood," "Shooting the Concubine," "Li Xianglian Sells Paintings," and "Returning the Cup." The content of the following seven operas needs to be revised: "Five Daughters Crying at the Grave," "Widow Ma Opens a Shop," "Butterfly Dream: Splitting the Coffin," "Pearl Shirt," "Embroidery as Matchmaker," "Obscene Mirror," and "Moral Retribution." The following two operas are prohibited from performance: "New Son-Killing Retribution" and "The Case of Liu Gong." Most of the operas were prohibited because the performers' singing and movements were close to lewd and offensive to public morals. Therefore, the Bureau has scheduled a meeting at 10:00 AM today at the Lecture Hall of the Municipal People's Education Hall on Wenmiao Road, summoning all Bang Bang Opera performers from the Empire Theatre and the North China Opera Theatre to provide guidance on the points that need improvement. All performers and playwrights must be present on time to receive instructions in order to achieve the desired improvements.

Li Jingfang Dies in Dalian - Dispute Over Inheritance - Concubine Accuses Li's Sons and Grandsons of Embezzlement - Trial Opens Yesterday, None of the Defendants Appear 113

Li Jingfang, also known as Bo Xing, the son of Li Hongzhang, the former Qing Dynasty Grand Secretary, withdrew from politics after the founding of the Republic of China and lived a secluded life in Dalian. Towards the end of the year before last, feeling his age, he summoned his sons and grandsons to his residence and personally wrote a document similar to a will, entrusting it to his eldest son, Guoqi, and grandsons, Jiaji and Jiazhui, for safekeeping. The document detailed how his assets should be distributed after his death, with the intention of preventing future disputes over the inheritance. In September of last year, Bo Xing died in Dalian. Initially, there were no problems among the family members. However, his concubine, Ms. Wu, who resided in Shanghai, only learned of his death this spring. She then discovered that the document written by Bo Xing clearly stated that 23,000 yuan should be allocated to cover her living expenses, as well as expenses for her old age, illness, and death. She went to Li's residence at No. 5, Kangle Village, Fuxu Road, to demand the money from Guoqi and his sons, but received nothing. Although she repeatedly sent letters to negotiate, she received no response. Ms. Wu, believing that Guoqi, Jiaji, Jiazhui, and their accountant, Zhou Mengwen, should not violate the will and embezzle her substantial funds, hired lawyers Zuo Dexi and Xu Yinru to file a criminal lawsuit against Li and others in the First Special District Court, accusing them of embezzlement. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu Yugui opened the court to summon the defendants, but none of them appeared. Lawyer He stated that he represented Li Guotao and Li Jiaxing, but Li Jiaji and Zhou Mengwen were in Nanjing and Wuhu, respectively, and Jiazhui was hospitalized due to lung disease, while Guoqi was occupied with other matters, so they could not attend the court. The court then questioned the plaintiff, Ms. Wu, who stated that she was 43 years old, resided at No. 5, Huanlong Road, and that the defendants had embezzled her 23,000 yuan for living expenses and future funeral expenses. She stated that she had demanded the money from them in January of this year, but the defendants claimed that the money had already been given to her. In reality, the defendants concealed the news of her master's death from her, and she only learned of it in January. The plaintiff's lawyer then summarized the indictment, stating that the document was written by Bo Xing for his sons and grandsons, and there was only one copy, which was not in the plaintiff's possession. The fact that the document instructed the payment of 23,000 yuan to the plaintiff was undisputed. The defendants claimed that the money had already been paid, but after the plaintiff's negotiations, Bo Xing's second son, Guotao's brother Guoxiao, sent a letter to Zhou Mengwen stating that the money should be paid, indicating that it had not been paid initially. Guoxiao is currently residing at the Sacred Heart Hospital on Ningguo Road, and it is requested that he be summoned to testify, and that the original document be subpoenaed for review. The defendant's lawyer argued that the case was of a civil nature and cited the recent order issued by the Ministry of Judicial Administration to prevent abuse of private prosecutions, requesting that the case be transferred to the civil court for resolution. Judge Liu then adjourned the hearing to the afternoon of December 11th to subpoena Li Guoxiao and order the defendants to bring the document to court for further examination.

Old Shanghai Exhibition Held at the International Academy of Dramatic Arts 114

At 5:15 PM the day before yesterday, the International Academy of Dramatic Arts held an Old Shanghai Exhibition on the top floor of the YWCA at No. 55, Yuanmingyuan Road. Over a hundred people attended, mostly members of the association. Dr. Finn, an elderly female medical doctor, gave a speech about her observations and experiences in Shanghai and Beijing, which was quite humorous. Dr. Finn came to China in 1884 and arrived in Shanghai during the 1911 Revolution, having lived in China for over 50 years. Several old Shanghai artifacts were displayed in the venue, especially various maps, which were particularly valuable. Among them was a map of the French Concession from 1832, which was quite rare. Xu Zhiqin, also known as Mao Mao, residing at No. 20, Lane 40, Yalu Road, Hongkou, is a beef merchant. Because he is good at flattery and dancing, he has accumulated some savings. However, starting on the 7th of this month, Xu received several more threatening letters, scheduling a meeting in front of the mortuary on Feilun Road. They secretly went to the mortuary on Feilun Road and waited several times, but did not see any bandits. In recent days, plainclothes officers had been seen near Xu's house. He confessed that he lived at No. 5, Yuezu Lane, Dongyouheng Road. Yesterday morning, the police station's lawyer, Zhang Shizhu, filed charges against him in the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court for attempted extortion under Article 346, Clause 3 of the Criminal Law. He stated that the defendant confessed in the police station that he wrote the other nine letters in addition to the previous three threatening letters. The letter paper confiscated from the defendant's residence was identical to the letters received by Xu. The defendant also wrote a note in the police station, and the handwriting was the same as the threatening letters received by Xu. Because accomplices were still at large, the police station requested an extension of the investigation. Xu Zhiqin also testified that he saw the defendant deliver the letter to the crack in his back door yesterday morning. When questioned, the defendant evaded the charges. Judge Xiao ruled that the case needed to be adjourned and ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody for further questioning in seven days.

The con artist Dai [Name Omitted], from Yangzhou, recently came up with an ingenious plan. He went to the Ying Shun Yuan Red Gang Garment Shop on Luxiangyuan Road, owned by Yin Shengjin, and negotiated an order for 100 sets of military uniforms. Tianquan Pavilion Calligraphy, Painting, Inkstone, and Fan Exhibition 122

The owner of Tianquan Pavilion is a prominent family from Zhejiang, with an addiction to antiquities and particularly skilled in appraisal. Now, at the urging of friends, he is displaying hundreds of pieces of calligraphy and painting masterpieces from the Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties from his collection. The exhibition will be held at the Lake Society at the intersection of Beijing Road and Guizhou Road, starting from November 29th of the lunar calendar, for a period of seven days. The displayed items are divided into two categories: for sale and not for sale. In addition to the works of famous artists from the Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties, the calligraphy and paintings also include dozens of screens and couplets in various styles of seal script and clerical script by his ancestor, Mr. Xu Shanlin, as well as portraits of famous people from past dynasties. Among the inkstones are dozens of exquisitely carved inkstones made by Zhao Mengfu, Gao Nanfu, Ding Longhong, and others. The fans include palace fans collected by the Qing imperial court and dozens of folding fans with calligraphy and paintings by various famous artists, all colorful and splendidly displayed, which are sure to increase the interest of the viewers. The elegant mounting and backing are particularly ingenious, truly a grand spectacle. Famous painters Liu Haisu, Wu Hufan, and Tang Dingzhi, Du Xiaofan, and others will attend at the appointed time and provide systematic commentary.

Overview of the Shanghai Match Industry (Continued) 127

— Edited by China Credit Information Institute

Sales Channels of Various Match Factories

The matches used in our country in the past were all imported by ship, as mentioned earlier. Regarding the sales volume in China, taking Swedish matches as an example, since 1921, the annual sales volume increased from 100,000 taels to 200,000, and then from 200,000 to 400,000 and 600,000. By 1930, it further increased to 1,010,000 taels. Examining the reasons for this increase, there are approximately two points: (1) Because foreign merchants used unequal treaties as protection, imported goods were exempt from customs duties and taxes, so they could dump goods everywhere without any concerns. (2) Because foreign merchants used the most-favored-nation clause to establish factories in China, saving on transportation costs and being able to offer lower wages, the cost was reduced, and they could compete with lower prices. In 1931, although the government increased the import tariff rate on matches, seemingly limiting the import of matches, the number of manufacturers in China increased, making it impossible to control them uniformly. The original power has not been reduced in the slightest, truly making them strong rivals to the Shanghai match industry. Therefore, when describing the sales channels of various match factories in Shanghai, one must first describe the market for Shanghai match factories and the situation of competition with foreign goods. Sales volume, taxes paid, and market prices are secondary.

1. Market: The match market in our country is extremely complex, with domestic matches, imported matches, and matches manufactured in China by foreign merchants. The distribution areas are roughly divided into five regions: the Jiangsu-Zhejiang-Anhui region and the Hunan-Hubei region are mostly within the sphere of influence of Chinese factories; the Shandong-Henan region is divided equally between Chinese and Japanese factories; the Guangdong-Guangxi-Fujian region is occupied by Chinese factories and Swedish merchants; the Jiangsu-Zhejiang-Anhui region is a battleground for Chinese factories, foreign factories, and importers. Currently, the sales channels of various factories in Shanghai, such as the Jiangsu-Zhejiang-Anhui region, are a gathering point. Within the region, the market is divided into six areas: one is Shanghai, Suzhou, and nearby ports; two is Nanjing, Zhenjiang, and the Jiangbei area; three is Xuzhou, Bengbu, and Linhuai; four is Wuhu and Anqing; five is the Ningbo-Wenzhou-Taizhou area; and six is Hangzhou, Jiaxing, and Huzhou. The area with the greatest market competition is Nanjing, because Shanghai matches are mostly gathered in Nanjing before being distributed to the Yangtze River area. 2. Competition from Foreign Goods: Foreign matches are divided into two types: imported goods and those manufactured in China. Among the foreign factories in Shanghai, only the Meiguang Factory has a large output and wide sales channels. In the past, it was mainly sold in Hankou and near Xiamen. Recently, due to heavy taxation in those areas, it has shifted to promoting sales in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, causing another factory's products to compete in the Jiangsu-Zhejiang-Anhui region. Among imported goods, Japanese, Russian, and Swedish goods are the most numerous. Russian "Tiger" brand matches were once dumped in China but have gradually decreased recently. Swedish matches have been imported the most over the years, and dumping is especially strong. There are a total of 27 trademarks registered at the Trademark Bureau, such as Spinning Wheel, Ruyi, God of Wealth, Flying Tiger, Zhong Kui, Alarm Bell, Rose, Temple, Three Mountains, Horseshoe, Golden Phoenix, etc. Among Japanese matches, "Bridge," "Monkey," and "Phoenix" brands have the widest sales channels. In the past, they were on par with Swedish matches, but due to the boycott of Japanese goods, sales have greatly decreased. Swedish matches took the opportunity to dump their goods, further affecting them. However, they still occupy a portion of the market. The import amounts of foreign matches in the past three years are listed below, according to the "Customs Sino-Foreign Trade Statistics Annual Report":

According to the table above, the total import amount of foreign matches in 1932 was 370,989 cases, in 1933 it was 72,976 cases, a decrease of 298,013 cases compared to the previous year, and in 1934 it was 109,756 cases, an increase of 36,780 cases compared to 1933, but still a decrease of 261,123 cases compared to 1932. Therefore, the decrease in imports of foreign matches in recent years is sufficient to help the progress of the domestic match industry. 3. Sales Volume: The sales channels of various match factories in Shanghai, in general, small factories mainly focus on this city and nearby ports. Factories with strong capital, such as Dahua and Meiguang, are distributed throughout Zhejiang and the Yangtze River area, in addition to the local market. In the past, sales were limited due to the dumping of Swedish matches. Since January 1931, after the increase in the import rate of matches, the import of foreign matches has decreased, and the sales channels of various factories have gradually become more active. In 1933, the government suddenly increased the high amount of consolidated tax, increasing the cost of various factories, and the sales price was higher, so sales were affected again. Up to now, there is still a downward trend. Looking at the sales volume of various factories in the past three years, one can see a glimpse of the decline of the match industry.

Factory Name 1932 (July to June) Cases 1933 (July to June) Cases 1934 (July to June) Cases Dahua Shanghai Rongchang Factory 25,620 26,197 23,964 Dahua Zhoupu Zhonghua Factory 28,202 20,285 14,616 China Factory 5,385 7,885 Unknown Daming Factory -- 2,640 Unknown Dahua Factory 10,181 8,059 Unknown Meiguang Factory 35,480 17,531 Unknown 4. Tax Payment: Match tax is based on a box as a unit, with each box containing six tins, each tin containing ten packs, and each pack containing twelve small packs, and each pack containing ten boxes. Boxes are divided into three types: A, B, and C. Type A is a small box, Type B is a medium box, and Type C is a large box. Currently, each box in Shanghai factories should pay consolidated tax: Type A is approximately 13.5 yuan in national currency, Type B is approximately 17.4 yuan, and Type C is approximately 21 yuan. After the manufacturers pay the tax, they can transport and sell the goods to various places, and the government does not levy additional taxes. If the sales location is not within the consolidated tax area, then taxes are paid according to the local tax regulations. All consolidated taxes previously paid by the manufacturers can still be requested from the government for reimbursement. 5. Market Price: In the past three years, the market price of Shanghai matches has fallen sharply due to the price reduction dumping of imported matches and the filling of the market with tax-evading matches. The average annual statistics show that the sales price per box in 1933 was approximately 36 yuan in national currency, and in 1934 it was approximately 30 yuan, a decrease of 6 yuan per box compared to the previous year. From January to June of this year, the sales price fell even more, with each box selling for only 26 yuan, a decrease of 4 yuan compared to 1934. In July and August, the price per box has risen to 28 yuan, but it is still 2 yuan less per box compared to last year. Recently, since the government implemented currency management, foreign exchange has increased, and raw material prices have gradually risen, increasing the cost of matches. Various factories are also planning to increase prices and are currently in consultation.

This year, the market price of matches is low, and competition from foreign goods is fierce. It is particularly difficult for various Chinese factories to operate in these difficult times. Fortunately, the industry is trending towards cooperation, seeking remedies together. Dahua Match Company has also jointly organized the National Match United Business Office with Dahua, Zhonghua, Daming, and other match companies in this city, as well as Da, Tongsui, Huai Shang, Minsheng, and Chu Sheng Match Companies in other cities, to control operations, standardize market prices, open up sales channels, and balance production and sales. This may not be the dawn of the match industry's future. (The End)

World Games Next August - Our Country Will Participate in Seven Events - Track and Field, Soccer, Basketball, Weightlifting, Race Walking, National Martial Arts, Swimming - Budgeted Expenses are 170,000 Yuan, Departure Planned for Next June 128

(Nanjing, 27th Dispatch) The Chinese National Sports Association has drafted a budget to participate in the 11th World Games, with planned events including soccer, track and field, basketball, weightlifting, race walking, national martial arts, and swimming. The training period will begin in March 1936, the departure date will be June 1936, the competition dates will be from August 1st to August 16th, and the return date will be in early September. The total budget is 170,000 yuan, with 30,000 yuan for preparation and training expenses. The round-trip ticket price from Shanghai to Berlin is 952 yuan per person. The round-trip second-class ticket from Shanghai to Venice is 32 pounds per person, and with each pound equivalent to 16 yuan in national currency, it totals 512 yuan. The round-trip second-class train ticket from Venice to Berlin is 66 lira (Italian currency) per person, and with each lira equivalent to 0.25 yuan, it totals 216 yuan. The Venice luggage tax is 9 pounds per person, and with each pound equivalent to 16 yuan, it totals 144 yuan. The tips on the train and ship are 80 yuan per person. The lodging and meals for the delegation in Germany for four weeks are 6 marks per person per day, totaling 202 yuan. The spending money for the delegation in Germany for four weeks is 56 yuan per day. The outfitting fee is 50 yuan per person. The domestic round-trip travel expenses for the delegation are calculated at an average of 100 yuan per person. The delegation will consist of 100 athletes and staff members (approximately 80 athletes and 20 staff members), totaling 136,000 yuan in national currency. The preparation fee is 10,000 yuan, the pre-selection and training expenses are 10,000 yuan, and the hospitality expenses for the delegation staff in Germany are 6,000 yuan, totaling 172,000 yuan in national currency.

Education News

Superintendent Zhong of the Ministry of Education Inspects - Report on Vocational Education in Zhejiang Province (2) 140

(4) Provincial Agricultural Vocational School (Acting on behalf of the Province)

The school has five classes for advanced agriculture and three classes for junior agriculture, with a total of 123 students. The enrollment method for advanced agriculture students is the same as for regular students. For junior agriculture, students are selected from designated counties, with qualified candidates being middle-level small landowners who are willing to farm themselves. Advanced agriculture students do not yet have summer assignments. Junior agriculture students have their holidays abolished. Everything except books is provided by the school. Huts are built to serve as places for residence and teaching. School workers are not used; students are responsible for cooking, washing, and cleaning to cultivate simple living habits and hard work. The equipment in the dormitories for advanced agriculture students is between that of universities and junior agriculture students. The dining hall and classrooms are in the same place as the university, and management and discipline are often affected by each other. Achievements in agricultural production and manufacturing are notable. The junior agriculture program is newly established, with no performance achievements yet. Recently graduated advanced agriculture students often work in other provinces, such as in rural cooperation projects, due to being trained by the Construction Department as agricultural extension workers. Most go on to further studies. In the past, most students found employment.

The first year of junior agriculture should focus on basic operations and cultivating diligent habits. The second year should focus on the economic concepts of agriculture and the mastery of planting techniques. The third year should focus on experimental improvement work and the use of new agricultural tools.

(5) Provincial Jinhua Experimental Agricultural Vocational School

The school's recent plan is to expand junior agriculture and temporarily suspend the enrollment of advanced agriculture students, if necessary.

The school has six junior classes with over 190 students. A few are graduates of junior high school or silk industry schools, but most are children of farmers. The students’ levels vary greatly, making teaching quite difficult. Group teaching methods should be adopted. Students with slightly higher levels can be assigned special materials or reference books to avoid the tedium of repetitive work. In the upper grades, outstanding students should be given leadership roles.

The school farm is about 200 mu. Achievements in ordinary crops are noticeable, but the farmland should be expanded to allow for sufficient practical experience. The equipment for all scientific and new agricultural tools is very simple, insufficient to satisfy the knowledge-seeking desires of upper-grade students and should be enriched urgently. The school’s atmosphere of simplicity is commendable, but it lacks cleanliness, lighting, and attention to hygiene, which may give students bad farming habits. The dining hall is orderly, and the food is cheap and delicious, managed by the students themselves, which can be used as a reference for other schools. Students do not have winter or summer vacations; they work and study half-time each day. The spirit of labor is good, but students are allowed to return to school to rest for 20 minutes around 3 PM. Students sometimes do not return to work in the fields on time and should be allowed to rest on the spot to save time.

(6) Provincial Training Institute for Agricultural Extension Personnel

The institute is run by the Construction Department, with 96 students recruited from junior high school graduates recommended by various counties. Expenses are borne by the counties, with self-funded students accounting for about half. After graduating in two years, they are assigned to agricultural and forestry farms for three months of probation before being assigned to various places as extension workers. Currently, there is no problem with their career prospects. They work and study half-time without winter or summer vacations. From plowing and fertilizing to harvesting, everything is done by the students. They are divided into five groups, each responsible for 100 mu of land, with each person responsible for about 5 mu. Another ten graduates are hired to assist and guide practical work. Teaching focuses on rice and wheat, followed by cotton, and then forestry and mulberry. However, due to the short period, they only have labor habits and general agricultural experience, without sufficient technology and knowledge. Practical guidance seems inadequate. It should be changed to three years to increase the cultivation of research and experimental abilities. The institute is comparable to the Zhejiang University Agricultural Experiment Farm and the Rural Teachers' Agricultural Farm. The purposes are similar, but the responsible authorities are completely unrelated. Cooperation should be sought to avoid repetitive work, to spend less money, and to achieve more effective results. Attention must also be paid to promoting rural cooperative enterprises.

(7) Zhuji County Junior Agricultural School

The school has three junior classes with over 80 students, mostly children of farmers. The farmland is 100 mu, with much wasteland, which does not conform to agricultural economic principles. Practical training is four hours per day, divided into two hours each in the morning and afternoon, which is inappropriate. This method may be used for first-year students who are young, but second and third-year students must concentrate their work to increase efficiency. When necessary, a 20-minute break can be taken in between to adjust. Vacation assignments should be implemented to avoid abandonment and waste. The annual holiday is slightly idle and can be given a two or three-week vacation. No attention has been paid to the marketing of agricultural products, and farmers still lack faith. There is a lack of new equipment, and there is no experimental work. The livestock farm is very unclean, failing to eliminate the bad habits of farmers.

The school receives a subsidy of 4,000 yuan from the Department of Education, and the local government raises about 4,000 yuan. If necessary, it should be taken over by the province to reorganize it.

(8) Provincial Ningbo Senior Industrial Vocational School

The school is divided into three departments: architecture and road construction, automobiles, and machinery, with a total of seven classes and 170 students. There are also two classes for craft supplementary studies, with a three-year graduation period and 40 students. The school was originally run by Ningbo County but was only taken over by the province last year. The equipment in each department is extremely simple. Although machinery students are required to practice for 24 hours per week, they actually only work for 12 hours in groups, which greatly affects their skills and must be improved urgently. Before there is sufficient equipment, the entire vacation time should be used for designated practical training to make up for it. Road surveying has not been linked with the Highway Bureau, and architecture has not been communicated with construction companies, lacking practical experience. Achievements are mediocre. More design and drawing should be done, as well as field visits and operational exercises, to seek the mastery of skills.

The supplementary classes work 10 hours a day and attend classes for 2 hours, learning subjects such as Mandarin, arithmetic, civics, physics, chemistry, and mechanical drawing. The workload should be reduced by two or three hours, and an outline of mechanical science should be added. If necessary, it can be converted into a junior school. The students' uniforms are very untidy, and the dormitories and classrooms of the supplementary classes are extremely messy and filthy, cultivating bad habits that should be improved. Judging from the past situation of the school, machinery students lack technical skills, fear hard work, and are lazy, with the worst career prospects. The situation can be considered, and elementary school graduates can be recruited and given five years of training. The first three years focus on technology, and the last two years focus on academic theory. Civil engineering, architecture, and supplementary classes have good career prospects. The textbooks for each department, such as surveying, machinery, and mathematics, should be changed to Chinese textbooks to increase efficiency. Furthermore, the affiliated Ningbo Factory should be combined with or merged into the school to provide practical training for machinery students.

Order from the Ministry of Education - Points to Note for Running Commercial Vocational Schools 141

The Ministry of Education issued a notice to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities on the 26th, stating, "Upon inspection, the establishment of public and private vocational schools in various regions should be based on local needs and the subjects offered should be specified. This has been repeatedly ordered by the Ministry in previous decrees. However, recently, newly established private vocational schools in various cities have considered commercial schools easier to run, and most are simple and inadequate, lacking a proper scale, which is very inappropriate. It must be known that for commercial vocational schools, everything from equipment to subjects and practical matters should be as perfect as possible. The actual needs of the vocational industry should be deeply studied to determine the teaching plan, so that students have real knowledge and experience, and can obtain corresponding positions after graduation. The following points should be noted when running commercial vocational schools: 1. The school bank must act as an agent for collecting student tuition and meal fees, and managing the payment of security deposits and meal fees, and encourage teachers and students to deposit money to increase practice opportunities. At the same time, the educational administrative organs should negotiate with several banks for observation and internship. 2. The school store must enrich its business content and types of goods, and strive for external business to increase practice convenience, not just limited to selling sweets and stationery. The store organization should also be handled in accordance with new procedures. Educational administrative organs should negotiate with several larger stores for students to practice after class. 3. Typing is an important technical subject and must be concentratedly trained, with as much equipment as possible. When necessary, post-class and holiday time should be used for supplementary practice, and learning time should not be delayed, or one day of cold, ten days of warmth. 4. The teaching of accounting and bookkeeping should collect as much practical material as possible, such as school revenue and expenditure numbers, for multiple exercises, with agility and accuracy as the main goal, not just seeking to understand the method, resulting in slow and erroneous procedures in practical application. 5. Each school must set up a complete commodity research room, collecting and displaying samples of Chinese and foreign goods for comparison, and supplementing them at any time for reference. Do not limit yourself to domestic goods, which will restrict knowledge to one corner. 6. The travel visits of graduating students must specify practical commercial problems in advance, group or individually collect materials, study facts, and after returning to school, prepare a systematic report for assessment. 7. Commerce focuses on general knowledge, so the teaching hours for English, Chinese, history, and geography can be more than those of other vocational schools. However, each school often overemphasizes general subjects, arbitrarily increasing teaching hours, so that commercial subjects take up very little time, which should be considered and reduced to match the name and reality. At the same time, English textbooks should be used as little as possible. 8. Each commercial school should encourage students to organize their own stores to cultivate the spirit of business enterprise, not just rely on the employment of existing banks and stores. 9. Most students in general three-year junior commercial schools do not wait to graduate, but instead work as apprentices and store clerks. The graduates often enter regular high schools, so the circumstances should be distinguished to shorten the time limit, or to run commercial vocational supplementary schools, and business leaders should be invited to organize an advisory committee to seek student career prospects. 10. In areas where the career prospects of commercial school graduates are not good, the educational administrative organs should restrict the establishment. When it is necessary to establish one, it should be concentrated. It is hoped that they will comply and instruct their subordinates to comply as well. This order."

The Education Bureau Formulates Teaching Progress Schedules - Each Group Held a Joint Meeting Yesterday - Scheduled to Convene Group Meetings - First Draft to Be Completed in January Next Year 142

In order to unify the teaching progress of all subjects in public and private middle schools in the city, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has established a committee for compiling teaching progress schedules for each subject in middle schools. Yesterday at 3:00 PM, the directors of each group of the committee held a joint meeting to discuss the compilation matters. The details are as follows:

Attending Members: The secretary of the committee, Chen Duanzhi, the director of the mathematics group, Wang Jimei, the director of the Chinese language group, Chen Youqin, the director of the physics and chemistry group, Shao Jialin, Zhang Youzhi from the foreign language group, the director of the biology and zoology group, Li Dihua, the director of the history and geography group, Zhang Yiyong, and the director of the civics group, Sun Letao, were all present. Zhang Youzhi chaired the meeting, and Chen Duanzhi recorded the minutes. First, the chairman reported the purpose of convening the joint meeting of the directors of each group, and then discussed the cases.

Resolved Cases: (1) Regarding the case of when the first group meeting should be held, it was resolved that the directors of each group should convene meetings separately before December 5th. (2) Regarding the case of determining the date of completion of the first draft, it was resolved that it should be completed by the end of January 1936. (3) Regarding the case of when the second joint meeting should be convened, it was resolved that it should be held at Wuben Girls' Middle School on January 5th, 1936. (4) Regarding the case of prescribing the formula for the progress schedule, it was resolved to follow the items decided by the full committee and request the Municipal Education Bureau to print and distribute them to each group for reference. (5) Regarding the case of whether the distribution of time for each subject should be slightly reduced based on the city's environment, it was resolved to comply with the curriculum standards. (6) Regarding the case of whether the drafting principles should be determined, it was resolved to determine the following principles: A. Use the week as the unit, B. Use simple materials as the main focus, C. Use the detailed items as the minimum, D. Pay attention to special local materials, E. Follow the standards promulgated by the Ministry as much as possible in the drafting order, F. Avoid repetition in the junior and senior high school materials. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Meeting of the Finance and Equipment Group of the Middle School Normal Education Research Association - Meeting of the Discipline and Military Training Group Today - Held at Lake Society at 4:00 PM 143

The Finance and Equipment Group of the Shanghai Middle School Normal Education Research Association held its first research meeting at the Lake Society on Guizhou Road at 4:00 PM yesterday. The first meeting of the Discipline and Military Training Group will also be held at the Lake Society at 4:00 PM today. The details are as follows:

Finance and Equipment Group: Attendees: Zhang Yi, Yan Zhenyu, Li Baozhen, Lu Songqian, Yan Junxuan, Cui Jianwu. Li Pengfei from the Municipal Education Bureau attended as an observer. Chairman: Zhang Yi. Recorder: Li Baozhen. Research questions: (1) How to establish school accounting procedure regulations. Result: Please each school adopt the following improvements as much as possible: Accounting system: (A) Adopt the new bookkeeping method, (B) The accountant and the general affairs officer must not be held by the same person, (C) Must have vouchers and deposit books, (D) Please ask an accountant to audit the accounts, (E) Establish an economic audit committee (its organization method is in accordance with the regulations issued by the bureau). (2) Request the Municipal Education Bureau to establish science experiment halls in each district. Result: Please the original proposer submit concrete methods for discussion at the next meeting, and please pay attention to the following matters: (A) How to divide the districts, (B) Equipment limit, (C) Detailed budget, (D) Source of funds. (3) Are there any difficulties in implementing the standards for the distribution of secondary education funds in each province and city stipulated by the Ministry of Education? Result: Whether there are any difficulties in implementing the standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education this time must be investigated first. It is proposed that the original proposer prepare an investigation form and send it to the bureau for approval and distribution to the educational administrative organs of each province and city for investigation and research. (4) How to reduce the burden on middle school students. Result: (A) Please public and private schools charge students as much as possible in accordance with the standards set by the Ministry of Education's middle school regulations, (B) Actively cultivate a frugal style of learning to reduce the burden, (C) Exempt all social donations. (5) Should the class teachers be required to have a specified salary to be responsible for their work? Result: Full-time teachers who serve as class teachers may be given a discretionary salary or reduce teaching hours by the school, but they must fulfill the duties of extracurricular guidance. (6) Research transferred from the 23rd case of the curriculum teaching group: There is a severe lack of excellent wall charts for junior high school biology, hygiene, history, and geography, and it is not easy for students to obtain clear concepts when teaching. Result: Please the central government pay attention to the preparation of various charts and graphs when compiling books for school use. (7) The next meeting is scheduled to be held at 4:00 PM on December 18th.

Discipline and Military Training Group: Held at 4:00 PM today. Members: Lin Meiyan, Zhong Xingbai, Jia Guanren, Shen Weizhen, Chen Bangyan, Zhang Shilin, Chen Mengyu, Tao Zailiang, Wang Xiyun, Guo Shouchun, Tang Zengyi, Huang Yiru. Research questions: (1) Promulgating a training plan for the period of national crisis, (2) Promoting practical cooperation between family and school, (3) How to improve the health of middle school students, (4) Should military management be implemented in middle schools, (5) The style and color of uniforms in middle schools in this city are different from those stipulated by the Directorate General of Training, how should this be resolved, (6) Should a separate dining system be adopted for students who board at school, (7) How to communicate the student self-government association with the Boy Scout organization, (8) How to promote moral education, (9) How to cultivate students' national thinking, (10) How should educational administrative organs assist in the implementation of military management to achieve it, (11) How to further rectify the school spirit, (12) The integration of discipline and teaching in middle schools, (13) How to revise the centralized military training time, (14) How to improve the effectiveness of discipline in middle schools, (15) How to prescribe middle school students' leave.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Man (1)(0)(8) 145

—Original by LouisaM. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"But, my dear, you are so tired and it is so hot, you won't be happy. Wait until I go with you, and we can go for a whole day and pick a big basket of wild berries and come back."

"You are always not going, you are always busy, I am tired of waiting. I would rather go and pick wild berries for you alone, I love this, I want to fill my new little bucket," Robert said with tears in his eyes.

Big teardrops fell into the lovely new little bucket as if it were not filled with blackberries, but with salt water—this sad scene deeply moved the women present. His mother gently patted his back, hoping that he would stop crying. Little Mei expressed her willingness to stay at home and accompany him; Donn, with his usual resolute attitude, said:

"Let him come; I will take care of him."

"If Fulan went, I wouldn't worry, because he is very careful; but he is helping his father mow the lawn now, and I can't trust the rest of you," Mrs. Pei began to say.

A guest suddenly interjected, "The road is too far."

"I would be willing to carry him if I went—but I can't go," Donn sighed.

"Thank you for your kindness, you still have to protect your feet. I wish I could go myself. Ah, I think we still have a way," Mrs. Pei said, and ran to the steps outside the door, waving her apron.

Yarn and Cotton: The Yarn Market Shows a Slight Decline, Near and Far Term Distance is Wide, But Dealers Sell on Rises 150

The yarn market is weakening, and the situation is slightly declining. The psychology of most dealers is that the price has reached a high level, so they take the approach of selling on rises. Moreover, there is sufficient delivery this month, and although buyers are prepared to accept all of them, it is not easy to sell them all at once. However, the stakes have increased. As for general non-industry players, because legal tender has a certain relationship with hard currency, the focus is on the long term, and the amount dragged in is still not released. Therefore, the line between near and far term prices is becoming increasingly distant.

Grain Prices: Flour and Wheat Markets Change Three Times in One Day — High Prices Attract Official Attention — 155

The flour market initially declined, then rose, and then fell again in the afternoon. Regarding foreign wheat quotations, both Chicago and Canada continued to fall by about 2-3 dimes. At the opening, foreign wheat quotations softened sentiment, falling about two cents compared to the previous day's closing price. Later, due to the factories not selling, large off-market players competed to buy, causing the market to rise steadily again. Prices for March and April rose nearly a cent compared to the previous day. When the market opened in the afternoon, it was initially stable. Later, it was heard that the social authorities, seeing the rapid price increases as endless and affecting people's livelihood, were conducting investigations to provide relief. Sentiment weakened again, and many bulls sold off, causing prices for all months to fall again by 2-3 cents. Currently, flour prices are already higher than rice prices. Although this is partly due to raw material costs, it is also partly due to market sentiment.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, 31-32 batches of goods arrived from various sources downstream. Transactions of various goods in the market were slow. Agricultural market prices slightly increased. Although there was some interest from hoarders in the afternoon, the scattered sales channels were stagnant, and prices remained stable. Traveler's Rice Prices Stabilize, Stockpiled Goods Revive 157

Yesterday, the demand for guest-style indica rice remained strong. In addition to rice from Hunan, Jiangxi, Ningbo, and Wenzhou, new rice from Fuzhou arrived. In recent days, both guest groups and local sellers have been quiet, and the market has been trending downward. The opening price in the morning was slightly lower by 2-3 cents. Investigation: October's Import and Export Status of Vegetables and Fruits 163

According to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, since the bureau began inspecting plant diseases and insect pests in July of this year, it has strictly cracked down on imported and exported plants with diseases and insects, especially vegetables and fruits. The purpose is to prevent the import of foreign diseases and pests, to protect domestic agriculture and the health of the people, and to prevent the export of plants with insects and bacteria, to enhance the reputation and sales development of domestic agricultural products in foreign markets.
