Shenbao National Products Weekly

Words of Contribution

Industry Self-Help 164

— Yang An

The position of national products industries today can be described as extremely difficult. I have heard many people involved in national product businesses say, "Running a national product factory is truly not something humans do. Tell our descendants not to run factories again and endure this suffering." Expressions of anger and resentment are everywhere. The current situation of national product industries, under such adverse circumstances, is truly a lamentable and painful reality. Therefore, many enthusiastic advocates of national products are concerned and planning for them, researching various proactive solutions. Some request reducing loan interest rates, some request promulgating regulatory laws, some request amending the real estate mortgage loan regulations, and some request accepting national product factories as collateral for loans. These are all hopes, after the promulgation of the new currency policy, that the government will utilize legal tender as much as possible to revitalize industry and commerce. I do not disagree with these opinions, but in all things, self-help is the only way to receive help from others. In the current situation, national product factories are characterized by internal strife and mutual jealousy. If they cannot unite spiritually, hoping for help from the government, banks, and the general public, in my view, there is no certainty of success. There is no need to discuss the distant past; even in the recent situation, since the implementation of the legal tender policy, companies still set prices individually, purchase raw materials on their own, meetings are merely formalities, proposals are ignored, public regulations are no match for private interests, and even industry rules and resolutions are violated, disregarding everything and prioritizing only personal interests. This is simply industry suicide, leading everyone to ruin. I simply cannot understand why the leaders of national product businesses are so short-sighted and narrow-minded. Despite the government's differing opinions and factional divisions over the years, the Fifth Plenary Session still showed a spirit of solidarity and unity to face the national crisis together. National product industries do not have any deep-seated grudges or inextricable relationships. Why, at this time of facing difficulties and being on the verge of ruin, can't they cooperate with one heart and mind, unite sincerely, and take action to help themselves? I believe that today's national product businesses can only survive through cooperation, and only self-help can prevent failure. Seeking help from others, from the government, or from society is not a solution, and it will not be effective. The national crisis deepens daily, and the situation is increasingly urgent. Everyone, rise up! Self-help for the industry.

Talking About National Paper Again 165

— Wen Bo

In the last issue, there was an article by Mr. Yihong entitled "Please the Printing Industry to Make Every Effort to Use National Paper," in which he described in detail the situation of various paper mills and the current attitude of various sectors of society towards using national paper. Now I will add some of what I know, regarding the situation of paper mills as follows: The Longzhang Paper Mill produces leather paper and white paper in addition to Lian Shi paper and Daolin paper. The Tianzhang Paper Mill may have the hope of resuming production even though it is temporarily suspended. In addition to Daolin paper, drawing paper, and writing paper, it also produces hair calendar paper, wood paper, blotting paper, Fu Shi paper, etc. Jiangnan Paper Mill produces Lian Shi, Mao Bian, Yu Kou, Chong Gong, and Hai Yue (is the most complete paper mill for making Chinese-style paper). Minfeng Paper Mill produces yellow cardboard, gray cardboard, and white cardboard, and also makes cigarette paper. Jingcheng Paper Mill, Dahua Paper Mill, and Huasheng Paper Mill all manufacture yellow cardboard. Senji Paper Mill, Shanghai Paper Mill, Baoshan Paper Mill, and Dazhonghua Paper Mill all manufacture Mao Bian Lian Shi and Hai Yue.

The products of the above companies are indeed very suitable for various types of printing, especially some products that are not inferior to imported products, such as Longzhang Daolin paper and Jiangnan Grade A Lian Shi.

As for the reason why domestic paper cannot be sold well, in addition to the reasons mentioned by Mr. Yihong, there are also several other reasons, that is, the raw materials of the above products, except for yellow cardboard, mostly use wood pulp from foreign countries. Therefore, the price of raw material costs is invisibly controlled by foreign merchants. The productivity of each paper mill is extremely low, which increases labor costs. The above two points are also the main reasons why domestic paper cannot be sold well.

Mr. Yihong also said that paper shops are unwilling to promote domestic paper, and printing houses do not use domestic paper to replace foreign paper, which is a cold attitude. However, I think this situation is not cold, what is even colder is that there are a group of paper shops and a group of printing houses; they clearly use or sell cheap and high-quality domestic paper, but they still say it is imported goods in front of their customers in order to gain huge profits. How many customers can truly distinguish domestic paper from foreign paper? They clearly use domestic products but do not know they are domestic products, and there are other situations such as using second-rate foreign goods to fill in for domestic products, etc. This kind of coldness is truly more ridiculous.

Most of the paper shops in Shanghai sell foreign paper. If you just walk past the doors of various paper shops, you can see signs such as "X Foreign Paper Company" and "X Foreign Paper Company." Therefore, the image of domestic paper in the minds of the general public is very shallow.

Recently, a Dafeng National Paper Company (on Qipan Street and Jiaotong Road) has appeared in this city. It is said that it specializes in selling domestic paper and does not sell a single sheet of foreign paper. I personally visited it once and it is indeed a pure domestic paper shop. The young clerks in the store are all full of energy, friendly in attitude, and constantly talk to customers about the country's economy and the benefits of using domestic goods. Moreover, in order to promote domestic goods, the store's prices are particularly cheaper than other stores. I am very happy to see this. This is truly a shining star in the domestic paper industry and I especially recommend it, hoping that the printing industry will cherish it.

Yu Jiesan Invented Fire Extinguishing Powder 166

— Linghu Zhao

China's progress in science and technology in recent years seems to be very slow on the surface, but in fact, it has special progress. There have been many small inventions emerging one after another.

I remember that I have introduced the inventions of Ms. Ding Yusan and others before. Today, I will introduce the fire extinguishing powder invented by Mr. Yu Jiesan from Northeast China. Mr. Yu spent several years of painstaking research and many experiments to create a complete fire extinguishing powder. According to Mr. Yu, "This powder is made by combining various substances containing carbon dioxide (CO2). It has a lasting fire extinguishing property. Its fire extinguishing ability does not disappear even after forty minutes, unlike ordinary ones." Indeed, this fire extinguishing powder has been proven by experiments to prevent extinguished fires from reigniting. Moreover, the powder absolutely does not contain acids or other substances, so there is no danger of corrosion or damage even if it comes into contact with the human body or valuables. Another point that is not comparable to other imported fire extinguishers is that when applied to burning oil, it can float on the surface and extinguish extremely violent flames.

Currently, Mr. Yu has obtained a patent from the Ministry of Industry and plans to establish an office in this city and set up a large-scale fire extinguishing powder factory to be used by the Chinese people. It is said that Mr. Yu has sent representatives Jin Yichen, Mei Ziying, and Shi Rongting to Shanghai a few days ago to discuss preparations with Mr. Shi Bingyan and other well-known Northeast merchants in this city.

Alarming Number of Imported Perfumes and Powders 167

— Meng Zhao

634313 Yuan

The numbers of the first prize of the China Aviation Highway Construction Lottery are of great concern to everyone before and after the lottery period! You could call it a fevered pursuit of wealth! Now the reporter has seized on the public's psychology of valuing wealth to write about this topic of "634313", so that everyone can pay a little attention! Be a little alarmed! Remember "634313", especially the ladies!

According to a report from the International Trade Bureau, "Shanghai's consumption of perfumes and powders in the first ten months of this year reached 6,343,130 yuan in national currency! The United States accounted for 1,318,030 Customs Gold Yuan, France 778,500 Customs Gold Yuan, the United Kingdom 632,600 Customs Gold Yuan, Japan 387,310 Customs Gold Yuan, Germany 340,210 Customs Gold Yuan, Hong Kong 104,470 Customs Gold Yuan, and other countries 35,630 Customs Gold Yuan, with a total value of 3,565,180 Customs Gold Yuan, equivalent to 6,343,130 yuan in national currency." In October alone, the number of imported perfumes and powders was 54,063 yuan in national currency... If 6,343,130 yuan were used to establish national product factories or to relieve the stagnant commercial market, at least it could achieve the prosperity of national products and recover a lot of rights and interests!

Alas! The effect of promoting national products for several years is like this! What else is there to say? But hope must always be hoped... Everyone should change their psychology and safeguard national product businesses. The authorities' decisive promulgation of the new currency policy is giving us one last test!

New Invention by a Chinese Person 168

— (Xiang Xian)

Huang Chao, a Chinese paper engineering graduate from Germany, has recently invented a type of smokeless gunpowder using chemical bamboo pulp. Its safety and blasting power are better than the existing cotton gunpowder. This invention is beneficial to China because China lacks cotton but is rich in bamboo. Dr. Babben, director of the Institute of Defense Chemistry at the Berlin Institute of Technology, believes that this product is a new discovery in the modern gunpowder industry and awarded Mr. Huang a special engineer degree, which is a very international honor.

National Product News in One Week

Shanghai industrial and commercial leaders Rong Zongjing, Liu Hongsheng, Guo Shun, Nie Lusheng, Yu Qiaqing, etc., requested that measures be taken as soon as possible to reduce loan interest rates and save industry.

The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau urged various industries to report on measures to prevent rising prices.

The hot water bottle industry is rectifying industry prices and has requested the competent authorities to find ways to stop silver nitrate raw material factories from hoarding and raising prices.

Imports of Chinese and foreign porcelain in nine months have exceeded 2.9 million Customs Gold Yuan, with products from Germany, the United Kingdom, and Japan being the most numerous.

The National Products Promotion Alliance presented eight items to the Ministries of Finance and Industry, requesting the promulgation of regulatory laws, accepting national products as collateral for loans, and using legal tender to revitalize industry and commerce.

The Vietnam Chinese National Exhibition will send personnel to contact and solicit national products.

Wang Zhisheng arrived in Beijing, presented suggestions to the government on improving national products, and requested that a national product exhibition be held in Nanyang.

The seasoning industry announced that prices would be increased across the board from November 25.

Leaders of national product factories, Ren Shigang, Fang Jiange, Li Kangnian, Xu Yangnan, Gao Shiheng, etc., traveled to Beijing together to promote their businesses.

The China Industrial National Products Trade Association specially formed an overseas promotion team, which plans to go to Nanyang next spring to promote products, and the implementation steps are in the planning stage.

The Ministry of Industry approved Tianli's light gas products, Guoxing Factory's lacquer, Da Zhonghua Automobile Tire, New Life Company's rayon, cellophane, and Zhejiang Minfeng Paper Mill's cigarette paper to enjoy exclusive manufacturing rights in Shanghai for five years.

Publishing Industry

"Spiritual Construction and National Revival" 169

— Ren Qian

By Zhou Fohai, New Life Edition (Price: 40 cents)

Today’s China is in a state of internal turmoil and external aggression, and as a result, “How to revive the nation” has become the central topic of discussion among insightful people in recent years. Some say that to revive the nation, we must first revive the countryside; some say that to revive the nation, we must first popularize education; and still others say that to revive the nation, we must reform the political system. In short, there are many different opinions and no consensus. Of course, reviving the countryside, popularizing education, etc., are indeed necessary tasks for reviving the nation, but because the entire nation does not have a common heart and a common goal; command cannot be unified, steps cannot be consistent, and efforts will be in vain. Therefore, the prerequisite for reviving the nation is how to unify the consciousness of the entire nation under the same goal, and then can generate collective great power. Mr. Zhou Fohai’s book "Spiritual Construction and National Revival" was written for this need.

This book is divided into five chapters, with the following table of contents: (1) The Meaning and Importance of Spiritual Construction, (2) Observing the Relationship between the Spirit of the Times and the Rise and Fall of the Nation from History, (3) The Evolution of Various Movements in Recent Decades and the General Cause of Their Failure, (4) The Goals of Spiritual Construction, (5) The Principles and Plans of Spiritual Construction.

The first chapter explains what spiritual construction is and its importance. He said: "We feel that spirit and matter are mutually beneficial. Completing spiritual construction is precisely to complete material construction. Because the elements of spirit are not fully equipped, and the conditions of spirit are not fulfilled, material construction cannot be completed at all." He also said: "The rise and fall of a nation, the decline of a dynasty, the rise and fall of a family, and the success or failure of a person, although the reasons are complicated and the conditions are numerous, cannot be explained by a monistic theory; however, the effect of the spirit can be said to be the fundamental reason and the main condition. When a nation is about to rise, a dynasty is about to flourish, a family is about to prosper, and a person's career is about to succeed, it must first have a spirit of vigorous advancement, perseverance, and courage. Conversely, when a nation is about to perish, a dynasty is about to decline, a family is about to decline, and a person's career is about to fail, it must first show a spirit of decadence and decline, laziness and romance, and cunning and falsehood."

The second chapter reviews the relationship between the spirit of the times and the rise and fall of the nation from Chinese history, and analyzes and studies in detail the four periods of the Wuhu Rebellion, the Five Dynasties Rebellion, the invasion of the Liao, Jin, and Yuan Dynasties, and the rule of the Manchu Qing Dynasty, which are cited as the most painful and shameful periods for the Han people; and the reason for causing this shame is nothing more than the deterioration of the social atmosphere and the decline of the spirit at that time.

The third chapter explores the causes of the evolution and failure of various movements in the recent decades since the Opium War and the invasion of imperialist forces into China. The main movements, such as the shipbuilding and weapon manufacturing movement, the reform movement, the democratic movement, and the new culture movement, were all very much in line with the needs of the time, but why did they fail in the end? Mr. Zhou said: "The fundamental reason for the failure of this movement is the lack of spiritual elements sufficient to make them successful. Not only the people who opposed these movements were mostly motivated by selfishness, but also the people who directly or indirectly participated in these movements, except for a very few leaders, also rarely possessed the spirit of great public interest and selflessness, and honesty and trustworthiness... Therefore, the great hope that each movement possessed at the beginning was shattered by the corrupt atmosphere of private gain, bribery, inertia, falsehood, reckless anger, and power struggle, and turned into a bubble." He also talked about the reasons for the failure of the New Culture Movement: "The nature of the New Culture Movement is the same as the movements in the above three periods, because it lacks the elements of the spirit, so it cannot complete the task that was hoped to be completed at that time; the New Culture Movement itself is a kind of spiritual construction movement, but also because the people who participated in the movement mostly lack a sound and pure spirit, so it cannot complete the mission it should bear. Breaking the cannibalistic etiquette was originally a necessary way to transform the old customs that were not in line with human nature and inhumanity, but some frivolous youths used this slogan to engage in promiscuity; developing individuality was also a way to reform the old-style education, but some unfilial students therefore advocated abolishing exams; others used the beautiful name of freedom and liberation to disobey social order and school discipline; or used the slogan of revolutionary resistance to oppose their fathers and brothers at home and expel their teachers at school; or took down idols as the reality, and slandered the respected predecessors whom they did not like. In short: except for a very few leaders and pure youths, most of them used the New Culture Movement as a banner to pursue their private gains. Therefore, the result of this movement, although it awakened some people to the shortcomings of the old society, and also broke some bad customs and habits, and even traditional ideas, however, even in terms of its good aspects, the results were all negative and destructive, without actively constructing a pioneering spirit and a new atmosphere. In other words, the New Culture Movement, although it itself is a spiritual construction movement, however, its result only achieved the destruction of the spirit, as for spiritual construction, it has not succeeded. Therefore, the task of reviving the nation that we hoped it would bear cannot be completed."

The fourth chapter puts forward the goals of spiritual construction: (1) To eliminate the atmosphere of harming the public for private gain and build a spirit of forgetting the self for the public. (2) To eradicate the atmosphere of perfunctoriness, coping, and hypocrisy, and build a spirit of loyalty to what one does and loyalty to one's duties. (3) To eradicate the atmosphere of mutual evasion and mutual blame, and cultivate the spirit of enduring hard work, enduring difficulties, enduring grievances, and bearing blame. (4) To eradicate the psychology of indifference and cultivate an atmosphere of enthusiasm. (5) To eradicate the atmosphere of individual freedom and cultivate the spirit of strict discipline. (6) To eradicate the bad habits of meanness and corruption, and establish an atmosphere of valuing reputation and integrity and emphasizing integrity.

With goals, there must be methods to implement them, so the last chapter of this book is to put forward the principles and plans of spiritual construction. In terms of principles, he stipulated two types, one is automatic, hoping that everyone will realize it themselves; the other is passive, that is, promoted by external forces. In addition to these two methods, I think we can also adopt a method of honor and punishment. If the goals of spiritual construction are violated, the group will issue a warning in the name of the group, because "everyone has a sense of shame and evil," which may have some effect on the negative side. The most important thing is naturally on the positive side. On the one hand, we should use school education to try our best to instill the meaning and importance of spiritual construction to students. On the other hand, we can use social education, such as public education halls, libraries, etc., to often hold lectures and performances to make it deeply rooted in the hearts of the people.

Finally, Mr. Zhou put forward several plans: (1) Leading figures should "lead by example" according to the goals of spiritual construction. (2) Talents should be employed according to the goals of spiritual construction. (3) The government's rewards and punishments should be clearly defined according to the goals of spiritual construction. (4) Social public opinion should be created according to the goals of spiritual construction. (5) Training should be carried out according to the goals of spiritual construction. These methods are of course the most practical and effective methods, but the most important thing, I think, is to change the social atmosphere. On the one hand, leaders should lead by example, and at the same time, the people should be united, and everyone should work hard, so that the work of national revival can be completed as soon as possible.

In short, this book is worthy of attention in the current stage of China. I hope that the publication of this book will have a great effect on the spiritual construction of the Chinese nation!

Introducing a Book on Anthropology 170

— Tan Fuzhi

I have read many books on anthropology before, but after reading them, I always have this feeling: human beings are the same as other lower animals, primitive and wild, completely living a life of natural growth. That is to say, in general anthropology books, we only see the most primitive human beings, completely subjugated to the laws of nature. It seems that human beings have not evolved, even if they have evolved, they have completely followed the law of pure biological evolution such as "survival of the fittest." In this way, then anthropology is also zoology. Moreover, it seems that in general anthropology books, we only see the display and comparison of the fossils of some excavated ancient humans, and we do not see a modern person, a living person. Moreover, the so-called human being is only an individual, not human beings—groups of people.

The book "System of Anthropology" (Xin Ken Bookstore Edition, by Liu Min) that I am introducing now is completely different. First of all, it "puts anthropology between natural science and social science," unlike the old anthropology, which is purely natural science. Because human beings are both a product of nature and a product of society. As long as they are human beings who have broken away from the animal stage, they must not only live in nature and take nature as their environment, but also must live in society and take society as their environment. Because of this reason, the evolution of human beings on the one hand follows the laws of nature—the laws of biological evolution, and on the other hand obeys the laws of social development. The more human beings evolve, the relatively smaller they are dominated by the blind laws of nature, and the relatively greater they are dominated by the laws of society. This book forcefully explains this point from a sociological point of view.

Based on this basic point of view, it puts forward "the unnatural factors and their laws in human physiological evolution." It says that animals only passively change their organs to adapt to nature, while human beings can develop external organs—tools—to change nature. "Society is something that reduces the authority of nature to dominate human physical organs, and it is a tool to transfer human physiological adaptation to the natural environment to the adaptation of external organs." When human beings reach here, their degree of evolution is not determined by the degree of physiological adaptation to nature, but by the productive forces of their society.

Animals' living materials are completely taken from nature, while "the living materials of human beings mostly depend on labor products, and their need for the help of their companions is far above that of animals." The social instinct of human beings to love groups "often expands due to the expansion of the scope of this economic life," so the psychological evolution of human beings mostly depends on society.

Therefore, this book gives a correct solution to the inheritance and environment problem that scholars have been arguing about. It believes that the inheritance of human beings cannot be viewed solely from the physiological aspect, but also from the social aspect, because society is the environment of human beings. The so-called instinct is only a function reflected from the past environment and accumulated by ancestors, and the reason why this function can be exerted and evolved depends entirely on the inducement and edification of the current environment. Therefore, it is wrong to talk about eugenics purely by using the method of artificial selection in biology. The main thing to do in eugenics is to improve the environment—especially the social environment. Moreover, the evolution of human beings is the evolution of groups, the evolution of society, and is definitely not the evolution of individuals or the evolution of biology. Therefore, eugenics should be to improve the human race by social selection. "The weak must be eliminated in biology, while in human beings, it depends on the responsibility that they can fulfill to society. Eliminating the weak who are beneficial to society is not only not a good way, but a harmful act; on the contrary, preserving the strong who are not beneficial to society is not only not a good way, but also a harmful act." Therefore, the imperialistic eugenics that claims that the white race is the darling of heaven does not understand anthropology.

Malthus's population theory is also based on the theory of old anthropology, and it uses the principle of "competition and natural selection" to explain human evolution. But human evolution has social laws other than the laws of biological evolution. "Human beings can produce themselves," while organisms cannot. "The abundance or scarcity of the supply of human living materials depends on the progress of productive forces. The efficiency of human reproduction and the standard of population increase also depend on whether productive forces are developed." "When the development of human technology reaches the point where it can change the natural environment, and those natural conditions imposed on human beings gradually show that they are powerless, the development of the population is even more likely to break through the natural limits."

In short, this anthropology, which is based on new theories and new methods, has raised anthropology from the position of descriptive science to explanatory science, and has also pointed out to human beings themselves that human beings not only obey the laws of nature, but have also changed and overcome the laws of nature; not only are they dominated by the laws of society, but they must also understand society and transform society according to the inevitable laws of society. Human beings have moved from necessity to freedom.

Bookstore Scenes (Continued) 171

— Li Hengzhi

It is not that there are no employees who have undergone modern training. Not to mention large bookstores such as Commercial Press, etc., such as Life Bookstore, the training of employees is very strict (this is probably the effect of vocational education), and the efficiency of employees seems to be better than other bookstores. It is said that most of the employees they hire have received considerable modern education, and there is no apprenticeship system. If there is, it is only a modern-style trainee. However, we know that in industrial organizations, the treatment of workers in capitalist management is sometimes worse than that in family workshops. It is said that the same situation also exists in the book industry.

The monthly income of bookstore employees is only 10 to 20 yuan, and even for female employees, although there is an extra expense for decoration, the remuneration is only 10 to 20 yuan. In this period of rice as expensive as pearls and firewood as expensive as cassia, it is naturally not enough to support parents and not enough to support wives and children. Therefore, few bookstore employees are content with their job, which makes the managers of various bookstores feel the pain of not having good employees to use. What is the way out for bookstore employees? If they do not change jobs, then they see the huge difference between the cost and price of books, and they want to be "bosses" by chance. Sometimes we see bookstores that only print one or two books, which is an attempt by employees to become bosses. Some are fortunate enough to succeed, and their achievements or gains are those existing small family-workshop-style bookstores. As for those like Zhou Quanping, the "young boy of Creation Society," who jumped from being an employee to becoming a writer, it is really not very common.

(6) Editor-in-Chief

We have said that the general manager is important in the new bookstore, but if compared with the editor-in-chief, then the editor-in-chief is the soul of the new bookstore. Originally, nominally speaking, most new bookstores are divided into two major parts: the business department and the editorial department. The editor-in-chief is the head of the editorial department, and his position is important enough. What's more, there are even more than this, that is, one: the initial purpose of opening many bookstores is to publish books, especially books used to achieve a certain purpose. How the business is is secondary. In this case, the editor-in-chief is the only soul of the bookstore. If the editor-in-chief's intention does not match the original purpose of opening the bookstore, then the bookstore is equivalent to nothing. Second, many bookstores, nominally, have an editorial department, and have several editors, but in reality, the so-called editorial department is only nominally existing. The work of several editors is no different from that of proofreaders. Naturally, all publication policies are determined by the editor-in-chief's intention alone.

Understanding the role of the editor-in-chief in the new bookstore, you can find clues for the publication trends of various bookstores. Generally, the decision of the book publishing policy of each bookstore has many factors, but the editor-in-chief's intention is always one of the biggest determining forces. For example, in its early days, Mr. Zhang of Kaiming, from the editor-in-chief of women's magazines to the backbone of new women, was bound to be more interested in women's issues. Therefore, the publication of books on this aspect is also particularly large. Later, Mr. Xia was in charge of the editorial department. Because he was a middle school teacher with history and experience, Kaiming was created as a bookstore for middle school students. The New Life Bookstore was presided over by Mr. Tao Fan, so the most books on Chinese issues and international politics and economics were published. The Dawn Bookstore has always been presided over by Mr. Sun Wu, so many books on political economy, especially university textbooks, and English literature books have been published. Before the gentlemen of the Yusi Society left Beixin, it was a famous publishing institution for literary books. Later, after Mr. Zhao took charge, the style changed. For example, Zhonghua, which was originally competing with the Commercial Press, has published new books in recent years, which are not too bad, but they are not unique. Among the types of publications, it seems that there are more books on education, which is naturally related to Mr. Shu. There are also editors-in-chief who have no preference and no expertise of their own. Their decisions on publishing are naturally inexplicable. When Datong expanded, it accepted a large number of Jing manuscripts. As a result, they were either not published, or few people wanted them after they were published, which of course had to be the responsibility of the editor.

It is not that there are no editorial departments that are responsible for reviewing the book publishing plans, but most of the new bookstores are not very large. Except for the editor-in-chief, there are not many bookstores with more than three editors (excluding proofreaders and "de facto" proofreaders). Even for bookstores with a slightly scaled editorial department, such as Kaiming, although there are many editors, the powers are always biased. The Commercial Press has the most detailed division of labor in the editorial department, but the final decision on whether to accept or reject books still lies with Mr. Wang. Therefore, even if we say that in the new bookstore, the editor-in-chief (including the general manager) is invariably the soul of the bookstore, it is not an exaggeration.

Because the position of the editor-in-chief is so important, various bookstores attach special importance to the selection of the editor-in-chief—no, in fact, the editor-in-chief of each bookstore has no so-called "selection." For bookstores that are opened for the purpose of publishing books, the editor-in-chief is naturally the founder of the bookstore. Otherwise, the editor-in-chief of each bookstore must be the person who has the closest relationship with the bookstore, such as major shareholders, directors, or confidants of the founder. Therefore, in many new bookstores, the general manager is often replaced, but the editor-in-chief is rarely changed.

Of course, we cannot fail to mention those purely commercial bookstores. In this type of bookstore, the boss or founder is mostly an outsider to the duties of the editor-in-chief, and few of their related people are insiders. Therefore, they have to consult outsiders. Because of the existence of this type of bookstore, there was a time when the editor-in-chief also became one of the goals of literati to compete for. Competing for the editor-in-chief is the same as officials competing for green seats. Many people use all kinds of base means, and even use political power to oppress the bosses of this type of bookstore. At that time, there were several "imperial commissioner" editors in several bookstores. Because of this, several bookstores had to change their editor-in-chief frequently, and several others closed their doors in the several changes of the editor-in-chief. Such as New Universe, etc., are victims under this situation.

If we purely stand on the position of the new book industry to judge the good or bad of the editor-in-chief, then what qualifications should the editor-in-chief possess? We believe that the editor-in-chief needs a relatively high academic foundation, but cannot have too deep prejudices, and should also have some understanding of the various departments of academics. It is better for a bookstore to hire a literati who has considerable common sense in all aspects than to hire an expert with particularly high academic knowledge but no general common sense. In addition, the editor-in-chief should not only consider the market relationship when publishing books, but also the academic value, and use academic influence to change the market relationship—that is, to create a scholarly atmosphere. (To be continued)

Leukorrhea and Bloody Leukorrhea 176

— (Female Physician Chen Jianmei)

Leukorrhea and bloody leukorrhea are diseases that are particularly common among Chinese women. Lack of proper care during menstruation, inadequate postpartum care, and the use of unclean hygiene products can all lead to diseases of the uterus and vagina. The result is increased inflammatory secretions. In mild cases, these secretions are yellowish-white and sticky, known as leukorrhea. In severe cases, ulcers develop in the internal mucous membrane, and superficial blood vessels are damaged, causing blood to mix with the secretions, known as bloody leukorrhea. Some cases of leukorrhea and bloody leukorrhea are caused by tumors in the cervix, others by venereal viruses, and still others by general weakness and emaciation, or acute and chronic simple diseases of the urinary and reproductive organs. Since there is a definite cause for the symptoms of leukorrhea and bloody leukorrhea, it is regrettable that women often delay seeking medical attention out of shame, allowing the condition to progress and become incurable. This is deeply lamentable. Treatment of Crural Ringworm 177

— (Physician Gu Zhenqun)

Crural ringworm, also known as red inguinal ringworm, often occurs in areas where the skin of the thighs rubs together easily. It is light red in color and is a type of chronic filamentous fungal infection. The causative agent of this disease is the *Epidermophyton floccosum*, a fungus discovered in 1895 by Bruhl-Linder. It is small in shape, only about one-third the size of the *Malassezia furfur* fungus. It forms dense networks and specifically proliferates between the corneal cells with specific characteristics, mainly occurring in the groin area and spreading to nearby areas. Like common stubborn ringworm, it is a persistent and itchy skin disease. This condition is more common in men in our country and can be transmitted to others. The most effective and reliable treatment is artificial sunlamp irradiation or external application of "Gan Lu" (Sweet Dew) medicinal lotion. If both are used simultaneously, the speed of effectiveness will be even more unexpected. This lotion is sold by Tong Ren Xi Yao She at No. 1 Dexing Lane, Xinxin Bridge Street, French Concession, Shanghai. The price is one yuan per bottle, with an additional two cents for postage outside of Shanghai. This medicine also has special effects on other skin diseases.

Self-Treatment for Spermatorrhea 178

— (Physician Zhou Kechang)

There are many methods for treating gonorrhea. However, this method is not suitable for self-treatment by patients unless under the direct guidance of a physician. This is because gonococci infect from the external urethra, and if self-treatment is not performed properly, it can cause the gonococci to penetrate deeper, leading to bladder and other diseases. The simplest and safest self-treatment method is for patients to wash the pus that flows out of the external urethral orifice, as well as the swollen foreskin and glans, with cold boiled water from time to time. Drink plenty of boiled water to promote urination and take bladder and urethral antiseptics, such as Urotropin and Salol. Avoid stimulating substances such as tobacco, alcohol, and spicy foods. Treatment for Acne and Freckles 179

— (Physician Chen Xingzhen)

Acne, commonly called "zhang luo," is more common in young people, with fewer cases in women than in men. Among young men, seven or eight out of ten suffer from it. When it occurs, numerous papules and pustules appear on the cheeks and forehead, gradually turning from red to black, containing rice-colored granules or bleeding. It can be painful and itchy and often recurs. Applying "Mian Li" (Face Beautiful) to this condition has remarkable effects and can prevent recurrence. "Mian Li" also has a special effect: it can treat freckles. It has always been thought that there is no specific medicine for freckles, and those who suffer from freckles often lament that there is no effective treatment. In particular, young women are always trying every means to remove them for the sake of beauty, but without success. In fact, freckles are caused by pigmentation in the skin, resulting in brown or black spots on the epidermis. "Mian Li" has the chemical action to remove these spots. The effect is particularly remarkable and has been proven repeatedly. Therefore, "Mian Li" has created a new record in the medical field and cannot be compared with ordinary beauty cosmetics.

Small Talk

Banter 181

— Zinan

According to reports in various evening newspapers on the 25th, the new residence of movie star Hu Die was falsely reported to the fire department, causing the fire department to make a fruitless trip. According to Pan Yousheng, "Recently, countless calls from the outside world have been received day and night, often consisting of jokes, which are truly unbearable."

From this brief news, we can at least see the following two points: First, the inexplicably wonderful fans suddenly felt disappointed in their beloved (not to mention cherished) star, so they retaliated. Due to the depth of their love, the means of retaliation exceeded the extent of "sour grapes" and turned into action. Furthermore, due to the general cowardice of the national character, the means of retaliation only reached the level of "banter." Second, the result of the star system in recent years is that the film industry has become a deformed development. The so-called "fans" love not the film but the star. Therefore, the every move of the movie star has become the center of attention for the fans. The details of their daily private life are endlessly inquired about, which is already enough to show their "loyalty." Once they get married, and the person they marry is not a film industry worker, it is naturally inevitable that there will be a commotion. The aforementioned "countless calls, often consisting of jokes" is enough to prove this.

Now let's talk about the so-called "banter" issue.

The so-called means of retaliation in our China have always been very pitiful. Little Sanzi was bullied by the strong and powerful Big Liuzi. Little Sanzi secretly wrote the words "Big Liuzi is a small cart" on the wall and door of Big Liuzi's house, considering it retaliation. Once the words "small cart" were written, he felt victorious in spirit. Old Man Ah Q also became the old man who was beaten by his son? So he loudly sang "I will beat you with a steel whip" and returned in triumph.

The false alarm at Hu Die's house, as well as the "countless times" of "banter" phone calls, are the legacy of Ah Q's spiritual victory.

Of course, the times are progressing, and Mr. Ah Q has also taken a step forward from the era of "being beaten by his son." He not only knows how to "win spiritually," but he can also make the other party suffer some minor pains, such as "false alarms."

However, this further "spiritual victory" is actually only a difference of fifty steps from a hundred steps. Mr. Ah Q has not changed his essence. Furthermore, if this continues, Mr. Ah Q will never be reborn.

Here, we are not encouraging revenge killings. I always feel that revenge killings are more bright and promising than "banter." Of course, personal heroism is fundamentally unfeasible now. Even if you can kill everyone, such a killing often leads to extremism and short-sightedness, making people only see a small corner of the world without seeing the whole picture. And what is the difference between banter and revenge killings, except that it is devoid of reason and full of prejudice?

The two are simply twins from the same parents except for the different means—both are the final set of tricks of a pitiful nation when their scheme is exhausted.

However, this pitiful nation is prevalent in this set of tricks of showing the dagger when the map is unrolled to the end. They squirt water on reason, are trapped by short-sightedness, and blindly engage in a momentary burst of activity with their eyes closed, without considering what it will accomplish in reality or what damage or threat it will pose to the enemy.

As for making a trap for themselves to jump into, "bantering" with movie stars is even more superficial and ridiculous.

Sound of Night Rain 182

— Hua Mu

Several consecutive days of gloomy weather are really making people feel a bit uncomfortable. When you look up and see the accumulated clouds in the sky, you immediately worry and dislike that it will rain. If it were winter, with such weather and a hunting north wind blowing outdoors, you could still shift your dull and bored mood to imagining the snow scene; or gather three or five friends by the warm stove, warm half a cup of hot wine, and pass the days with chatting and laughing. However, it is still late autumn and early winter now. In this Jiangnan area, it is not yet time for snow. The accumulated clouds in the sky will definitely cause rainy days.

Rain only gives me annoyance. My reason for disliking rain is very simple. If I were now living in a city street in Shanghai, with a thoroughfare asphalt road right outside the window, I might be able to leisurely lean on the glass window and admire the street scene in the rain when it rains. This is just a small town on the outskirts of Shanghai. Rainy days only make this small town lonely and deserted, and the roads are also muddy and difficult to walk on. People can only stay in the house all day, listening to the ticking eaves dripping and enduring every second and minute with a bored mood, and can't help but feel how difficult it is to endure these idle days. Everything has become illusory and unreliable, intangible. If it is sunny, this small town can show its inherent beauty: the wild grass-covered fields, the green and verdant vegetable plots, the leaves of the maple trees and tallow trees that have changed color, the boatmen floating on the river, the morning glow, the evening glow, the cloud shadows, and the sounds of birds, all of these scenery are enough for me to linger and savor, giving me a temporary intoxication, washing away the shadows of life that are depressed in my heart; and when I am tired of reading in the morning, evening, or middle of the day, I can sit leisurely by the door with a cup of boiled water, listening to the voices of the hawkers walking in and out of the alley, or the creaking sounds of the small carts outside the fence; or stand by the lamppost at the entrance of the alley, watching the dust of the cars speeding away and disappearing into the groves, I feel that the air in this small town is harmonious and fresh, and it should give me some days of reclusive life in this ordinary way.

But the rain that destroys the beauty of this small town has finally fallen, starting in the afternoon with waves of

Page 16

Falling, the sky seems to be getting lower. Until now, when I am about to take off my clothes and rest in the middle of the night, the alley and the road outside the fence are cold and deserted. The wonton peddlers who knock on the clapper and pass by the alley entrance at lighting-up time every night, the shouts of selling sandalwood olives, the wild dogs madly chasing pedestrians, and the sound of cars, have all become silent, and no sound can be heard anymore, as if these sounds had never agitated in this small town.

If it just calms down like this, I think it will only give me a short-term feeling of loneliness at most. At this time, it is late at night, and I have to hide in bed to rest anyway, and it will definitely not be as boring as staying in the house during the day, making the days long and boring. Unfortunately, the situation is not so smooth. I really can't help but complain that the west wind this autumn is too lenient. Autumn has reached its final season, although it is said to be the Jiangnan area, the leaves of the plane trees should have fallen long ago (didn't the ancients have the poem "The grass and trees wither in Jiangnan at the end of autumn"), but what is happening now, the leaves of the several French plane trees planted next to the fence are hanging unharmed on the branches, making a disturbing and complicated sound tonight.

Before I fall asleep, will these two sounds stop? I am really worried in my heart. I can't help but think of Li Yishan's famous line "Leaving the sound of residual lotus and the sound of rain", which probably refers to listening to the complicated sound of autumn rain hitting the residual lotus leaves at night. This is originally an extremely elegant and unrestrained clear interest, which non-refined people cannot appreciate. If I slightly understood this kind of clear interest, then tonight's rain hitting the plane trees could be enjoyed with tranquility, and maybe I would even stir up poetic thoughts and write one or two poems or prose pieces recording the facts.

But unfortunately—actually, it is ashamed, I am ultimately a profit-seeking person, and the bitterness of life has long corroded my mood and changed its color. Because of these two sounds, I can't help but think of the muddy road tomorrow, the kind of difficult road that is waiting for me to trek through in a tangible or intangible way, whether far or near!

Alas, tonight's sound of rain, I can only sigh a big sigh at it.

Debt Collection 183

— Le Jian

—One of the City Chronicles.

Carrying a worn-out baggage and stepping on the smoky haze of the seasons, I wandered outside for many long years; I was greedy for the life of the wild, and then I carried a tired heart and hurried back to the mountain city, full of the thought that there would always be some clear days.

The dawn light in the mountain city probed out from the dust, and the last rays of the setting sun also withdrew into the dust. The table and chairs wiped very clean cannot withstand the accumulation of dust and are quickly covered with a thick layer of dirt. Every time I luckily sell a package of insecticide or a bottle of styptic medicine, I record the account in the dust-covered long bench. But I quickly came to feel the dryness of watching the door of the store, and I needed the scenery of the mountains and the fresh air.

On this day, my fourth uncle handed me a receipt book and asked me to collect some old debts along the way and told me the route. He also told me whether the houses of the debtors were thatched or brick, and a set of words to use when collecting debts. I set off early in the morning, carrying a large bunch of bright red lychees, and also picked a willow branch on the road to make a sun hat.

Walking on the winding mountain path, the rocks and streams were vigorous, the pines and plank bridges were splashing ink, the mountain city was still throwing it self in the distance between the mountains, and it was as silent as a tomb.

It was not that I was rushing on the mountain path, but that the mountain path was stretching out its rugged and endless body, asking me to patiently pursue the village at the end, ridiculing me. Finally, I was inevitably tired, and my heart was filled with a few points of wandering resentment.

When the lychees in my hand were peeled, I began to set foot on the cobblestone village road. What welcomed me enthusiastically was a nest of wild honeybees and a swarm of mosquitoes from the cattle shed like locusts. What awaited me calmly was a narrow and desolate alley and countless dilapidated walls. I read the names of the people on the receipt book one by one, going from door to door.

I knocked on the moldy wood doors, called out outside the earthen garden, or leaned against the broken walls to wait, and urged while sitting next to the weaving. But family after family, what I was able to collect was not the medicine bill, but a pile of nagging requests and complaints.

"Sir, you are an understanding person: when people contract smallpox, they only burn two sticks of incense in front of the Bodhisattva, and they will be fine in a short time. After taking two doses of your medicine, it almost killed the child in a few days... It was Guanyin Bodhisattva who saved him!"

"We shouldn't have called the doctor at that time. Tiger scratches are a common occurrence; how is a large bottle of styptic medicine as effective as a pinch of green silk smoke? Not to mention anything else, I think that bottle of medicine is just white water mixed with red cinnabar, it's very rare."

Listening to these unclear words, I just remained silent, dragging the shadow on the earth wall and walking away; I turned a corner and walked into a desolate alley.

Three oak-tiled houses, two old black lacquered doors, were originally the home of rich people. The fourth uncle had cured a man, and the bill in the receipt book had been written for a long time.

I stood outside the door and looked straight in, but I didn't see anyone. I gently knocked on the door knocker, but I didn't see anyone. It was as gloomy as walking into a funeral home. Finally, I called out:

"Hey! Is there anyone guarding the house? The Western medicine store in the city wants to settle some accounts."

Gradually, I saw the sound of iron chains clanging in the厢房. I took two steps back.

With a "ya" sound, the room door opened suddenly, and a middle-aged woman appeared in the room. Her clothes were torn to shreds and ragged, her hands and feet were in shackles, and her two jackal-like red eyes stared at me madly, her mouth blocked, as if she wanted to rush towards me.

"Huh! You came at the right time, go to his coffin to collect debts! Debt collector, you come, you come!" She shouted hoarsely, recklessly grabbing a three-legged stool and throwing it over, almost splitting my head open. I ran away.

From a distance, I could still hear the horrifying roar, unable to suppress a string of thumping heartbeats.

On the way back, I thought of the mad woman and the story of martyrdom.

Suzhou Ballad 188

Xia Hesheng's "Three Smiles"

Dun Ben (800) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening "Faded Red"

Official boats moored by the river bank. The rustling autumn wind is bitterly cold. The wise governor of Jiangzhou is seated above. During the feast, the wine is quite spirited. At that time, the honored guests and host are seated in a circle. And also, songs, odes and poems were offered for laughter and talk. Just then, a woman on a neighboring boat was particularly graceful. All that was heard was the interrupted sound of a pipa being played. Who knew? The old autumn beauty was still enchanting. And, the sound was delicate and wonderfully uncommon. It was said that the name of "Faded Red" (花褪紅) meant seeing guests with boundless shame. Before the honorable guests, she lowered her head without a word. Try to ask about it from the beginning. She said, "Since childhood, I have leaned on the door selling my charm. Never leaving dancing fans and singing robes. Then came a desolation without carriages and horses. Looking back, there is no home to return to. Therefore, I married as a wife. My husband went to Fuliang and has not yet returned. This caused me to be a lonely goose without a companion. Only specially, with old skills, do I seek food and clothing. It is only because of a meager livelihood and a difficult family situation. It is not because of my ill-fated beauty. I pity my own circumstance and disgrace my hairpins." Unexpectedly, it attracted the tears of the Jiangzhou Sima. Tear stains faintly wet his blue shirt. Originally, he was a passionate and talented man. His heart broke and his soul faded with two sighs. He did not begrudge rewarding her with heavy money. The horses and attendants returned, and the night was late. Lighting a lamp, unable to sleep, he was bored. He composed "Pipa Lament" and his tears were not yet dry. Outside the window, a curved remnant of the setting sun.

Hui Ling (1380) 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM

Opening "A Vain Female Student"

The mountains and rivers of Wulin are a spectacular sight. Talented people emerge from this blessed land. The maiden's face is like a celestial being. She has already completed her high school studies. Her heart is exquisitely clever. She likes the two words "vanity" the most. Her family does not worry about clothing, food, housing, or transportation. Her parents are old and enjoy meditation. She is regarded as a pearl in their palms and is spoiled. At home, she studies with her parents. In her childhood, she was betrothed to a fellow villager. He is a skilled painter and a teacher. He is kind and honest and has no worldly ambitions. His family is poor, but his intentions are extremely broad. The two of them are in harmony and go out together. They frolic among the Six Harmonies Pagoda and the Three Temples. In the setting sun, they hold hands and return. Their affection is sincere. Hoping that they can soon become a couple. Talented man and beautiful woman join in harmony. Bystanders sigh and admire. They all say, "A talented man and a beautiful woman are a match made in heaven." Good things are often ruined by fate. Suddenly, the situation changes and disaster arises. Originally, the maiden met a handsome young man. He has a doctorate and his surname is Han. Moreover, his father holds a high position in politics. He possesses both wealth and honor, and his reputation is renowned. She dislikes the painter's scholarly attitude. She completely abandons their past promises. With the doctor, they are as sweet as honey. They often boat together on West Lake. At this time, their passion is hot and their wedding date is set. The former Xiao Lang is like a stranger. Who knew? The doctor's heart is unpredictable. He suddenly forgets old friendships and falls in love with a new love. He actually abandons the maiden without news. Separating the loving couple, it is truly heartbreaking. Therefore, female vanity, you must not be greedy.

Movie News

Yi Hua News 191

"Song of Triumph" Nearing Completion

Bu Wancang's latest masterpiece, with Wu Weiyun as the photographer, Fang Peilin as the set designer, Gu Zongyi as the sound recorder, and starring Yuan Meiyun, Wang Yin, Wei Heling, Qin Tong, Wang Guilin, Jiang Xiu, Liu Li, and Li Junpan, Zhu Tianhong, etc., the Yihua all-dialogue sound and singing film "Song of Triumph" (totaling eighty-eight characters), which is set against the background of drought and depicts the plight of rural areas and the miserable lives of farmers, has been largely completed under day and night work. Now only one scene of the dam opening remains, and then the entire project can be completed.

The characteristic of this drama is not only that the script is realistic and the subject matter is novel, but also that the plot is tortuous and bizarre, and the scenes are extremely magnificent, tragic, stimulating and powerful. Therefore, it is said that "Song of Triumph" is indeed a great domestic film worthy of attention.

"Wedding Night" Discovers New Talent

Lin Ling is a brand-new newcomer, a newcomer who has been discovered by Yihua Company and is suitable for romantic roles. Currently, she has been assigned to be one of the main actors in Yue Feng's "Wedding Night." She plays a romantic and unrestrained modern urban woman, a standard fashionable girl who only knows how to dress up, dance, watch movies, and visit theaters, and does not know what is called womanly virtue or what is called love. She only boasts about youth and only regards being charming as a treasure. According to Yue Feng, she is indeed a promising talent and a surprising discovery. At the same time, "Wedding Night" can also be actively carried out without hindrance.

"Movie Life" and "Hu Die Wedding Special" 192

Xia Mingyi and He Zuoming co-edited the fifth issue of "Movie Life," which was published today. The cover is Li Lili in hunting gear, exquisitely printed in three colors. The text includes works by Yuan Meiyun, Huang Naishuang, Huang Hou, Mei Lin, Huang Ying, Liang Saisan, Mei Xiao, Ying Yunwei, etc. There are dozens of copperplate pictures, all of which are very valuable. In order to increase readers' interest, those who purchase a copy of "Movie Life" and cut out the special gift coupon from that issue will receive a set of the latest original photos of twelve major stars: Chen Yan Yan, Yuan Meiyun, Li Lili, Xu Lai, Chen Boer, Ye Qiuxin, Li Minghui, Hu Ping, Li Zhuozhuo, Huang Naishuang, Mei Lin, and Yuan Shaomei, totaling four large frames. The general distributor is the Shanghai Magazine Company on Fourth Road, and all major bookstores are authorized to sell it.

The 48th issue of "Electric Sound" published today has answers to questions such as how does Mr. Pan Yousheng's sister's Western friend support Mr. Pan? How to open a dance hall? What is the relationship between Hu Shan's friend, Mr. Liang? How did Hu Die meet Pan Lang? How was Lin Xuehuai with Pan? How did Hu and Pan fall in love? How does Pan Yousheng tolerate and serve Hu Die? There are also very interesting "pre-wedding interviews" and "special highlights of the wedding" records and other inside secrets, even Hu Die and Pan Yousheng themselves do not know. Available at all bookstores and newsstands, or send five cents for postage to Sanhe Publishing House, No. 138 Nanjing Road, and a copy will be sent immediately.

Daming Screens "Long Live Love" 193

The song and dance blockbuster "Long Live Love" Here is to Romanec, which once caused a sensation in the United States, is now scheduled to be released at the Daguangming Grand Theater starting today. The film is the debut work of modern opera master Niero Martini, which tells the story of a singer's private life and his love history. In addition to Annie Thoros, who played the Fairy Queen in "A Midsummer Night's Dream," it also hired world-renowned dance star Maria and Spanish dance king Ascota Iluk to participate in the performance at a huge cost. The film includes famous Italian songs, Spanish waves, the romantic atmosphere of Paris, and the beauties of Hollywood. Martini's singing voice is indeed like knocking on gold and jade. After the song king Carpanso, I'm afraid no one can compare to him. Moreover, the lingering and tragic plot is even more touching. In short, this is a unique song and dance blockbuster, which is indeed worth seeing. Some people say that it is enough to overwhelm "Song of Love", and it is not without reason. On the left is a scene of dance star Maria's toe dance.
